     1→import { useEffect } from 'react'
     2→import './App.css'
     3→
     4→const features: { id: string; icon: string; name: string; color: string }[] = [
     5→  { id: 'analytics', icon: '#',  name: 'Shared Analytics',  color: 'coral'  },
     6→  { id: 'calendar',  icon: '@',  name: 'Content Calendar',  color: 'teal'   },
     7→  { id: 'tasks',     icon: '+',  name: 'Task Board',         color: 'navy'   },
     8→  { id: 'ideas',     icon: '!',  name: 'Idea Inbox',         color: 'yellow' },
     9→  { id: 'assets',    icon: '=',  name: 'Asset Library',      color: 'green'  },
    10→  { id: 'goals',     icon: '^',  name: 'Goal Tracker',       color: 'purple' },
    11→]
    12→
    13→const STARS  = '★  '.repeat(60)
    14→const SPACER = Array(12).fill('★').join(' -=- ')
    15→
    16→const SPARKLE_COLORS = ['#FFD700', '#FF5533', '#007B7B', '#1A1A6E', '#FF9900']
    17→
    18→export default function App() {
    19→  // Sparkle trail
    20→  useEffect(() => {
    21→    let last = 0
    22→    let ci = 0
    23→
    24→    const onMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
    25→      const now = Date.now()
    26→      if (now - last < 90) return
    27→      last = now
    28→
    29→      const el = document.createElement('div')
    30→      el.className = 'sparkle'
    31→      const size = 6 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 6)
    32→      el.style.cssText = `
    33→        left: ${e.clientX - size / 2}px;
    34→        top:  ${e.clientY - size / 2}px;
    35→        width:  ${size}px;
    36→        height: ${size}px;
    37→        background: ${SPARKLE_COLORS[ci % SPARKLE_COLORS.length]};
    38→      `
    39→      ci++
    40→      document.body.appendChild(el)
    41→      setTimeout(() => el.remove(), 600)
    42→    }
    43→
    44→    window.addEventListener('mousemove', onMove)
    45→    return () => window.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMove)
    46→  }, [])
    47→
    48→  return (
    49→    <>
    50→      {/* Top star band */}
    51→      <div className="star-band" aria-hidden="true">{STARS}</div>
    52→
    53→      {/* Hero */}
    54→      <div className="hero">
    55→        <p className="hero-welcome">* * * WELCOME TO * * *</p>
    56→        <h1 className="hero-title">PABOPHER</h1>
    57→        <hr className="hero-rule" />
    58→        <p className="hero-desc">
    59→          A collaborative content dashboard for two creators sharing one channel.
    60→        </p>
    61→        <div className="hero-badges">
    62→          <span className="badge badge-new">NEW!</span>
    63→          <span className="badge badge-made">By Pab + Opher</span>
    64→        </div>
    65→      </div>
    66→
    67→      {/* Divider */}
    68→      <div className="pixel-divider" aria-hidden="true">{SPACER}</div>
    69→
    70→      {/* Features */}
    71→      <section className="features">
    72→        <h2 className="features-heading">FEATURES</h2>
    73→        <div className="features-grid">
    74→          {features.map((f) => (
    75→            <div key={f.id} className={`card card-${f.color}`}>
    76→              <div className="card-icon">{f.icon}</div>
    77→              <div className="card-name">{f.name}</div>
    78→            </div>
    79→          ))}
    80→        </div>
    81→      </section>
    82→
    83→      {/* Divider */}
    84→      <div className="pixel-divider" aria-hidden="true">{SPACER}</div>
    85→
    86→      {/* Footer */}
    87→      <footer className="footer">
    88→        <span>PAB + OPHER</span>
    89→        <span className="footer-sep">*</span>
    90→        <span>EST. 2026</span>
    91→        <span className="footer-sep">*</span>

    94→      </footer>
    95→
    96→      {/* Bottom star band */}

Good. I have a clear picture of the whole project. Here's the plan before I write a single line:

**What we're doing:**
1. Install `firebase` + `react-router-dom`
2. Restructure `src/` into `pages/`, `components/`, `context/`, `firebase/`
3. Move current landing page content to `src/pages/Landing.tsx`
4. Rewrite `App.tsx` as the router shell
5. Write `AuthContext`, `ProtectedRoute`, `Login`, and a Dashboard placeholder
6. Add login-page styles to `App.css` (matching the existing 90s aesthetic)
7. Create `.env.local.example` as a template (the real `.env.local` you fill in yourself)

**Auth approach:** Email/password only. No sign-up UI — you'll create both accounts directly in the Firebase Console. Session persists automatically via Firebase's default localStorage persistence.

Let's go. Installing packages and writing files in parallel:

  "content": "import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from 'react'\nimport type { ReactNode } from 'react'\nimport { onAuthStateChanged } from 'firebase/auth'\nimport type { User } from 'firebase/auth'\nimport { auth } from '../firebase/config'\n\ninterface AuthContextValue {\n  user:    User | null\n  loading: boolean\n}\n\nconst AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextValue>({ user: null, loading: true })\n\nexport function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {\n  const [user,    setUser]    = useState<User | null>(null)\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const unsub = onAuthStateChanged(auth, (u) => {\n      setUser(u)\n      setLoading(false)\n    })\n    return unsub\n  }, [])\n\n  return (\n    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, loading }}>\n      {children}\n    </AuthContext.Provider>\n  )\n}\n\nexport function useAuth() {\n  return useContext(AuthContext)\n}\n"
}

${e.clientY - size / 2}px;\n        width:  ${size}px;\n        height: ${size}px;\n        background: ${SPARKLE_COLORS[ci % SPARKLE_COLORS.length]};\n      `\n      ci++\n      document.body.appendChild(el)\n      setTimeout(() => el.remove(), 600)\n    }\n\n    window.addEventListener('mousemove', onMove)\n    return () => window.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMove)\n [tool_use: Write]
{
  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/pages/Login.tsx",
  "content": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'\nimport type { FormEvent } from 'react'\nimport { signInWithEmailAndPassword } from 'firebase/auth'\nimport { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom'\nimport { auth } from '../firebase/config'\nimport { useAuth } from '../context/AuthContext'\nimport '../App.css'\n\nexport default function Login() {\n  const [email,    setEmail]    = useState('')\n  const [password, setPassword] = useState('')\n  const [error,    setError]    = useState('')\n  const [busy,     setBusy]     = useState(false)\n  const navigate                = useNavigate()\n  const { user, loading }       = useAuth()\n\n  // Already logged in \u2014 go straight to dashboard\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!loading && user) navigate('/dashboard', { replace: true })\n  }, [user, loading, navigate])\n\n  async function handleSubmit(e: FormEvent) {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    setError('')\n    setBusy(true)\n    try {\n      await signInWithEmailAndPassword(auth, email, password)\n      navigate('/dashboard', { replace: true })\n    } catch (err: unknown) {\n      const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Login failed'\n      // Surface a clean message instead of the raw Firebase error\n      if (msg.includes('invalid-credential') || msg.includes('wrong-password') || msg.includes('user-not-found')) {\n        setError('Wrong email or password.')\n      } else {\n        setError(msg)\n      }\n    } finally {\n      setBusy(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (loading) return <div className=\"auth-loading\">LOADING...</div>\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"login-page\">\n      <div className=\"login-box\">\n        <h1 className=\"login-title\">PABOPHER</h1>\n        <p className=\"login-sub\">CREW ACCESS ONLY</p>\n\n        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className=\"login-form\">\n          <label>\n            EMAIL\n            <input\n              type=\"email\"\n              value={email}\n              onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}\n              required\n              autoComplete=\"email\"\n              spellCheck={false}\n            />\n          </label>\n\n          <label>\n            PASSWORD\n            <input\n              type=\"password\"\n              value={password}\n              onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}\n              required\n              autoComplete=\"current-password\"\n            />\n          </label>\n\n          {error && <p className=\"login-error\">{error}</p>}\n\n          <button type=\"submit\" disabled={busy} className=\"login-btn\">\n            {busy ? 'LOGGING IN...' : 'LOGIN >>'}\n          </button>\n        </form>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"
}

}

--- CLAUDE ---
All done. Here's a walkthrough of exactly what was built and what you need to do to activate it:

---

## What was built

**New folder structure:**
```
src/
  firebase/
    config.ts          ← Firebase init, exports auth + db
  context/
    AuthContext.tsx    ← onAuthStateChanged, useAuth() hook
  components/
    ProtectedRoute.tsx ← redirects to /login if not authed
  pages/
    Landing.tsx        ← your existing homepage (now at /)
    Login.tsx          ← email/password form
    Dashboard.tsx      ← placeholder (just shows who's in)
  App.tsx              ← now just the router shell
```

**Route map:**
| Path | What happens |
|---|---|
| `/` | Landing page |
| `/login` | Login form; if already authed → redirects to `/dashboard` |
| `/dashboard` | Protected; if not authed → redirects to `/login` |
| `/*` | Catch-all → `/` |

**Session persistence:** Firebase handles this automatically via localStorage. Refresh the page, still logged in.

---

## Steps you need to take before `npm run dev` will work

**1. Create a Firebase project** (if you haven't)
- Go to [console.firebase.google.com](https://console.firebase.google.com)
- New project → enable **Authentication** → Sign-in method → **Email/Password**
- Create two users manually (one for you, one for Pab) — no registration flow needed

**2. Get your config values**
- In the Firebase console: Project Settings → Your apps → Web app → copy the config object

**3. Create `.env.local`** in the project root (it's gitignored):
```
cp .env.local.example .env.local
```
Then fill in each `VITE_FIREBASE_*` value from the Firebase config object.

**4. Enable Firestore** (optional now, but you'll need it soon)
- Firebase Console → Firestore Database → Create database → Start in test mode for now

**5. Run it:**
```
npm run dev
```

That's the full auth foundation. When you're ready to start building the actual dashboard UI, we wire up the features against Firestore.

     1→import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
     2→import type { FormEvent } from 'react'
     3→import { signInWithEmailAndPassword } from 'firebase/auth'
     4→import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom'
     5→import { auth } from '../firebase/config'
     6→import { useAuth } from '../context/AuthContext'
     7→import '../App.css'
     8→
     9→export default function Login() {
    10→  const [email,    setEmail]    = useState('')
    11→  const [password, setPassword] = useState('')
    12→  const [error,    setError]    = useState('')
    13→  const [busy,     setBusy]     = useState(false)
    14→  const navigate                = useNavigate()
    15→  const { user, loading }       = useAuth()
    16→
    17→  // Already logged in — go straight to dashboard
    18→  useEffect(() => {
    19→    if (!loading && user) navigate('/dashboard', { replace: true })
    20→  }, [user, loading, navigate])
    21→
    22→  async function handleSubmit(e: FormEvent) {
    23→    e.preventDefault()
    24→    setError('')
    25→    setBusy(true)
    26→    try {
    27→      await signInWithEmailAndPassword(auth, email, password)
    28→      navigate('/dashboard', { replace: true })
    29→    } catch (err: unknown) {
    30→      const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Login failed'
    31→      // Surface a clean message instead of the raw Firebase error
    32→      if (msg.includes('invalid-credential') || msg.includes('wrong-password') || msg.includes('user-not-found')) {
    33→        setError('Wrong email or password.')
    34→      } else {
    35→        setError(msg)
    36→      }
    37→    } finally {
    38→      setBusy(false)
    39→    }
    40→  }
    41→
    42→  if (loading) return <div className="auth-loading">LOADING...</div>
    43→
    44→  return (
    45→    <div className="login-page">
    46→      <div className="login-box">
    47→        <h1 className="login-title">PABOPHER</h1>
    48→        <p className="login-sub">CREW ACCESS ONLY</p>
    49→
    50→        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="login-form">
    51→          <label>
    52→            EMAIL
    53→            <input
    54→              type="email"
    55→              value={email}
    56→              onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
    57→              required
    58→              autoComplete="email"
    59→              spellCheck={false}
    60→            />
    61→          </label>
    62→
    63→          <label>
    64→            PASSWORD
    65→            <input
    66→              type="password"
    67→              value={password}
    68→              onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
    69→              required
    70→              autoComplete="current-password"
    71→            />
    72→          </label>
    73→
    74→          {error && <p className="login-error">{error}</p>}
    75→
    76→          <button type="submit" disabled={busy} className="login-btn">
    77→            {busy ? 'LOGGING IN...' : 'LOGIN >>'}
    78→          </button>
    79→        </form>
    80→      </div>
    81→    </div>
    82→  )
    83→}

**Route map:**
```

/app                → redirects to /app/dashboard
/app/dashboard      → Dashboard placeholder  (protected)
/app/pipeline       → Pipeline placeholder   (protected)
*                   → redirects to /
```

**Shell layout** (`/app/*`):

┌─ PABOPHER ───────────────────── pab@x.com  [LOGOUT] ─┐  ← navy header
├──────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────┤

│   PIPELINE   │                                       │

**What adding a new protected page looks like** (one line each):
1. Create `src/pages/NewPage.tsx`
2. Add `<Route path="newpage" element={<NewPage />} />` inside the `/app` route in `App.tsx`
3. Add a `NAV_ITEMS` entry in `AppLayout.tsx`

--- YOU ---
Let's build the Video Pipeline feature for real. Each video card needs: title, platform (YouTube, IG Reels, or TikTok) current stage (Idea / Scripting / Filming / Editing / Published), creator tag (Pab or Opher), notes field, and a due date. I also want drag and drop between stage columns, and an overdue visual indicator on any card where the due date has passed. Store everything in Firestore. Start with the data model and Firestore helper functions before touching the UI.

--- CLAUDE ---


--- CLAUDE ---
Good call — data model first, UI second. Let me think through the shape before writing anything.

**Key decisions:**
- `dueDate` stored as `'YYYY-MM-DD'` string (maps directly to `<input type="date">`, trivial overdue comparison, no timezone weirdness)
- `createdAt` / `updatedAt` use Firestore `serverTimestamp()` — authoritative clock
- Flat `videos` collection (no subcollections needed for a 2-person private tool)
- `subscribeToVideos` uses a real-time `onSnapshot` listener, not one-off fetches — both users see each other's changes immediately without refreshing
- `updateVideo` handles both edits AND drag-drop stage changes (moving a card = `updateVideo(id, { stage: newStage })`)

Types first, then helpers:

  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/firebase/videos.ts",
  "content": "import {\n  collection,\n  doc,\n  addDoc,\n  updateDoc,\n  deleteDoc,\n  onSnapshot,\n  query,\n  orderBy,\n  serverTimestamp,\n  Timestamp,\n} from 'firebase/firestore'\nimport type { DocumentData, QueryDocumentSnapshot } from 'firebase/firestore'\nimport { db } from './config'\nimport type { Video, VideoInput } from '../types/video'\n\nconst COL = collection(db, 'videos')\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Firestore \u2192 app type conversion \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nfunction fromDoc(snap: QueryDocumentSnapshot<DocumentData>): Video {\n  const d = snap.data()\n  return {\n    id:        snap.id,\n    title:     d.title     ?? '',\n    platform:  d.platform  ?? 'YouTube',\n    stage:     d.stage     ?? 'Idea',\n    creator:   d.creator   ?? 'Pab',\n    notes:     d.notes     ?? '',\n    dueDate:   d.dueDate   ?? '',\n    createdAt: (d.createdAt as Timestamp | null)?.toMillis() ?? Date.now(),\n    updatedAt: (d.updatedAt as Timestamp | null)?.toMillis() ?? Date.now(),\n  }\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Real-time subscription \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Subscribes to the full videos collection, ordered by creation date.\n * Both users see each other's changes in real time.\n * Returns the unsubscribe function \u2014 call it in useEffect cleanup.\n */\nexport function subscribeToVideos(onChange: (videos: Video[]) => void): () => void {\n  const q = query(COL, orderBy('createdAt', 'desc'))\n  return onSnapshot(q, (snap) => {\n    onChange(snap.docs.map(fromDoc))\n  })\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 CRUD \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Creates a new video document.\n * createdAt and updatedAt are set server-side.\n */\nexport async function addVideo(input: VideoInput): Promise<void> {\n  await addDoc(COL, {\n    ...input,\n    createdAt: serverTimestamp(),\n    updatedAt: serverTimestamp(),\n  })\n}\n\n/**\n * Updates any subset of a video's fields.\n * Used for both full edits and drag-drop stage changes:\n *   updateVideo(id, { stage: 'Editing' })\n */\nexport async function updateVideo(id: string, changes: Partial<VideoInput>): Promise<void> {\n  await updateDoc(doc(COL, id), {\n    ...changes,\n    updatedAt: serverTimestamp(),\n  })\n}\n\n/**\n * Permanently deletes a video document.\n */\nexport async function deleteVideo(id: string): Promise<void> {\n  await deleteDoc(doc(COL, id))\n}\n"
}

No unauthenticated writes.\n    match /videos/{videoId} {\n      allow read, write: if request.auth != null;\n    }\n\n  }\n}\n"

Here's everything that was built and why each decision was made:

---

## Data layer summary

**`src/types/video.ts`**
- `Video` interface — the canonical app-side shape
- `VideoInput` — `Omit<Video, 'id' | 'createdAt' | 'updatedAt'>` — what callers pass to `addVideo`
- `STAGES`, `PLATFORMS`, `CREATORS` arrays — single source of truth for dropdowns and column ordering
- `isOverdue(video)` — compares `dueDate` to today at midnight (so a card due today is not overdue until tomorrow)

**`src/firebase/videos.ts`**
| Function | What it does |
|---|---|
| `subscribeToVideos(cb)` | Real-time `onSnapshot` — both users see changes instantly. Returns unsubscribe fn for cleanup. |
| `addVideo(input)` | Creates a doc, sets `createdAt`/`updatedAt` via `serverTimestamp()` |
| `updateVideo(id, changes)` | Partial update — handles both full edits and single-field drag-drop: `updateVideo(id, { stage: 'Editing' })` |
| `deleteVideo(id)` | Deletes the document |

---

## Before building the UI — one manual step

Paste the contents of `firestore.rules` into **Firebase Console → Firestore → Rules** and publish. This locks the database to authenticated users only and closes the test-mode open access.

---

Ready to build the Pipeline UI whenever you are — kanban columns, drag-and-drop, the add/edit form, and the overdue indicator.

  "content": "import type { Video, Platform } from '../../types/video'\nimport { isOverdue } from '../../types/video'\n\nconst PLATFORM_CLASS: Record<Platform, string> = {\n  'YouTube':  'platform-youtube',\n  'IG Reels': 'platform-ig',\n  'TikTok':   'platform-tiktok',\n}\n\nfunction formatDate(iso: string): string {\n  // 'YYYY-MM-DD' \u2192 'MM/DD/YYYY'\n  const [y, m, d] = iso.split('-')\n  return `${m}/${d}/${y}`\n}\n\ninterface Props {\n  video:  Video\n  onEdit: (video: Video) => void\n}\n\nexport default function VideoCard({ video, onEdit }: Props) {\n  const overdue = isOverdue(video)\n\n  return (\n    <div\n      className={`video-card${overdue ? ' is-overdue' : ''}`}\n      draggable\n      onDragStart={(e) => {\n        e.dataTransfer.setData('videoId', video.id)\n        e.dataTransfer.setData('sourceStage', video.stage)\n        e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move'\n      }}\n    >\n      <div className=\"video-card-title\">{video.title}</div>\n\n      <div className=\"video-card-meta\">\n        <span className={`platform-badge ${PLATFORM_CLASS[video.platform]}`}>\n          {video.platform}\n        </span>\n        <span className=\"creator-tag\">{video.creator}</span>\n        {overdue && <span className=\"overdue-badge\">OVERDUE</span>}\n      </div>\n\n      {video.dueDate && (\n        <div className={`video-card-due${overdue ? ' overdue-text' : ''}`}>\n          DUE: {formatDate(video.dueDate)}\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {video.notes && (\n        <div className=\"video-card-notes\">{video.notes}</div>\n      )}\n\n      <button className=\"video-card-edit-btn\" onClick={() => onEdit(video)}>\n        EDIT\n      </button>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"
}

  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/components/pipeline/KanbanColumn.tsx",
  "content": "import { useState } from 'react'\nimport type { Stage, Video } from '../../types/video'\nimport { updateVideo } from '../../firebase/videos'\nimport VideoCard from './VideoCard'\n\ninterface Props {\n  stage:      Stage\n  videos:     Video[]\n  onEditVideo: (video: Video) => void\n}\n\nexport default function KanbanColumn({ stage, videos, onEditVideo }: Props) {\n  const [isDragOver, setIsDragOver] = useState(false)\n\n  async function handleDrop(e: React.DragEvent) {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    setIsDragOver(false)\n    const videoId     = e.dataTransfer.getData('videoId')\n    const sourceStage = e.dataTransfer.getData('sourceStage')\n    if (videoId && sourceStage !== stage) {\n      await updateVideo(videoId, { stage })\n    }\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"kanban-column\">\n      <div className=\"kanban-column-header\">\n        <span>{stage.toUpperCase()}</span>\n        <span className=\"kanban-column-count\">{videos.length}</span>\n      </div>\n\n      <div\n        className={`kanban-column-body${isDragOver ? ' drag-over' : ''}`}\n        onDragOver={(e) => e.preventDefault()}\n        onDragEnter={() => setIsDragOver(true)}\n        onDragLeave={(e) => {\n          // Only clear when actually leaving the column \u2014 not when entering a child card\n          const related = e.relatedTarget as Node | null\n          if (!related || !e.currentTarget.contains(related)) {\n            setIsDragOver(false)\n          }\n        }}\n        onDrop={handleDrop}\n      >\n        {videos.map((v) => (\n          <VideoCard key={v.id} video={v} onEdit={onEditVideo} />\n        ))}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"
}

  "content": "import { useState } from 'react'\nimport type { FormEvent } from 'react'\nimport { PLATFORMS, STAGES, CREATORS } from '../../types/video'\nimport type { Video, VideoInput } from '../../types/video'\nimport { addVideo, updateVideo, deleteVideo } from '../../firebase/videos'\n\ninterface Props {\n  initial: Video | null  // null = add mode, Video = edit mode\n  onClose: () => void\n}\n\nconst EMPTY: VideoInput = {\n  title:    '',\n  platform: 'YouTube',\n  stage:    'Idea',\n  creator:  'Pab',\n  notes:    '',\n  dueDate:  '',\n}\n\nexport default function VideoForm({ initial, onClose }: Props) {\n  const [fields, setFields] = useState<VideoInput>(\n    initial\n      ? {\n          title:    initial.title,\n          platform: initial.platform,\n          stage:    initial.stage,\n          creator:  initial.creator,\n          notes:    initial.notes,\n          dueDate:  initial.dueDate,\n        }\n      : EMPTY\n  )\n  const [busy,  setBusy]  = useState(false)\n  const [error, setError] = useState('')\n\n  function set<K extends keyof VideoInput>(key: K, value: VideoInput[K]) {\n    setFields((prev) => ({ ...prev, [key]: value }))\n  }\n\n  async function handleSubmit(e: FormEvent) {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    if (!fields.title.trim()) { setError('Title is required.'); return }\n    setBusy(true)\n    setError('')\n    try {\n      if (initial) {\n        await updateVideo(initial.id, fields)\n      } else {\n        await addVideo(fields)\n      }\n      onClose()\n    } catch (err) {\n      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Something went wrong.')\n      setBusy(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  async function handleDelete() {\n    if (!initial) return\n    if (!confirm(`Delete \"${initial.title}\"? This cannot be undone.`)) return\n    setBusy(true)\n    try {\n      await deleteVideo(initial.id)\n      onClose()\n    } catch (err) {\n      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Delete failed.')\n      setBusy(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Close on backdrop click\n  function handleOverlayClick(e: React.MouseEvent) {\n    if (e.target === e.currentTarget) onClose()\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"modal-overlay\" onClick={handleOverlayClick}>\n      <div className=\"modal-box\">\n        <h2 className=\"modal-title\">{initial ? 'EDIT VIDEO' : 'ADD VIDEO'}</h2>\n\n        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>\n          <div className=\"form-field\">\n            <label className=\"form-label\">TITLE</label>\n            <input\n              className=\"form-input\"\n              value={fields.title}\n              onChange={(e) => set('title', e.target.value)}\n              placeholder=\"Video title\"\n              autoFocus\n            />\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"form-field\">\n            <label className=\"form-label\">PLATFORM</label>\n            <select\n              className=\"form-select\"\n              value={fields.platform}\n              onChange={(e) => set('platform', e.target.value as VideoInput['platform'])}\n            >\n              {PLATFORMS.map((p) => <option key={p} value={p}>{p}</option>)}\n            </select>\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"form-field\">\n            <label className=\"form-label\">STAGE</label>\n            <select\n              className=\"form-select\"\n              value={fields.stage}\n              onChange={(e) => set('stage', e.target.value as VideoInput['stage'])}\n            >\n              {STAGES.map((s) => <option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>)}\n            </select>\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"form-field\">\n            <label className=\"form-label\">CREATOR</label>\n            <select\n              className=\"form-select\"\n              value={fields.creator}\n              onChange={(e) => set('creator', e.target.value as VideoInput['creator'])}\n            >\n              {CREATORS.map((c) => <option key={c} value={c}>{c}</option>)}\n            </select>\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"form-field\">\n            <label className=\"form-label\">DUE DATE</label>\n            <input\n              type=\"date\"\n              className=\"form-input\"\n              value={fields.dueDate}\n              onChange={(e) => set('dueDate', e.target.value)}\n            />\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"form-field\">\n            <label className=\"form-label\">NOTES</label>\n            <textarea\n              className=\"form-textarea\"\n              value={fields.notes}\n              onChange={(e) => set('notes', e.target.value)}\n              placeholder=\"Any notes...\"\n            />\n          </div>\n\n          {error && <p className=\"form-error\">{error}</p>}\n\n          <div className=\"modal-actions\">\n            {initial && (\n              <button\n                type=\"button\"\n                className=\"btn-danger\"\n                onClick={handleDelete}\n                disabled={busy}\n              >\n                DELETE\n              </button>\n            )}\n            <button type=\"button\" className=\"btn-secondary\" onClick={onClose} disabled={busy}>\n              CANCEL\n            </button>\n            <button type=\"submit\" className=\"btn-primary\" disabled={busy}>\n              {busy ? 'SAVING...' : initial ? 'SAVE' : 'ADD VIDEO'}\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </form>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"
}

  "content": "import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'\nimport type { Video } from '../types/video'\nimport { subscribeToVideos } from '../firebase/videos'\nimport KanbanBoard from '../components/pipeline/KanbanBoard'\nimport VideoForm   from '../components/pipeline/VideoForm'\n\nexport default function Pipeline() {\n  const [videos,     setVideos]     = useState<Video[]>([])\n  const [editTarget, setEditTarget] = useState<Video | null>(null)\n  const [showAdd,    setShowAdd]    = useState(false)\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    return subscribeToVideos(setVideos)\n  }, [])\n\n  const isFormOpen = showAdd || editTarget !== null\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"pipeline-page\">\n      <div className=\"pipeline-toolbar\">\n        <h2 className=\"pipeline-heading\">VIDEO PIPELINE</h2>\n        <button className=\"btn-primary\" onClick={() => setShowAdd(true)}>\n          + ADD VIDEO\n        </button>\n      </div>\n\n      <KanbanBoard\n        videos={videos}\n        onEditVideo={setEditTarget}\n      />\n\n      {isFormOpen && (\n        <VideoForm\n          initial={editTarget}\n          onClose={() => { setShowAdd(false); setEditTarget(null) }}\n        />\n      )}\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"
}

--- CLAUDE ---
Done. Here's a full breakdown of what was built and how each piece works:

---

## Component tree
```
Pipeline.tsx
  ├── subscribes to Firestore via subscribeToVideos (real-time)
  ├── KanbanBoard  ← renders all 5 columns
  │     └── KanbanColumn × 5  ← one per stage, is the drop target
  │           └── VideoCard × n  ← draggable, shows overdue state
  └── VideoForm (modal, mounted only when open)
```

## How drag-and-drop works
1. `VideoCard` sets `videoId` + `sourceStage` on `dataTransfer` at drag start
2. `KanbanColumn` accepts the drop, reads those values, calls `updateVideo(id, { stage })`
3. Firestore's `onSnapshot` fires → `setVideos` → UI re-renders — no local state juggling needed
4. The `onDragLeave` handler uses `contains(relatedTarget)` to avoid flickering when dragging over child cards inside the same column

## Overdue logic
`isOverdue()` in `src/types/video.ts` compares `new Date(dueDate)` to today at midnight — so a card due today shows as not overdue until tomorrow. Cards trigger: coral border, bold red date, blinking `OVERDUE` badge.

## VideoForm modes
- **Add mode:** `initial={null}` — shows "ADD VIDEO" heading, no delete button
- **Edit mode:** `initial={video}` — pre-fills all fields, shows DELETE button (with `confirm()` guard) on the left, SAVE on the right
- Backdrop click closes without saving

---

Load the app, hit `/app/pipeline`, and click `+ ADD VIDEO` to test it end-to-end.

--- YOU ---

Show both options and the current votes. Second, when a card is moved to Published, trigger a brief confetti animation and increment a shared streak counter that tracks consecutive Fridays where both creators had a published video. Third, a live video URL field that appears only on Published cards. Fourth, a performance card that unlocks once the live URL is pasted, just three fields for now: views, likes, and one note. Keep all of this in Firestore. Build one at a time starting with title testing."

     1→// ── Enums / union types ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     2→
     3→export type Platform = 'YouTube' | 'IG Reels' | 'TikTok'
     4→export type Stage    = 'Idea' | 'Scripting' | 'Filming' | 'Editing' | 'Published'
     5→export type Creator  = 'Pab' | 'Opher'
     6→
     7→// Ordered — used to render columns left-to-right
     8→export const STAGES: Stage[]     = ['Idea', 'Scripting', 'Filming', 'Editing', 'Published']
     9→export const PLATFORMS: Platform[] = ['YouTube', 'IG Reels', 'TikTok']
    10→export const CREATORS: Creator[]  = ['Pab', 'Opher']
    11→
    12→// ── Core model ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    13→
    14→export interface Video {
    15→  id:        string    // Firestore document ID
    16→  title:     string
    17→  platform:  Platform
    18→  stage:     Stage
    19→  creator:   Creator
    20→  notes:     string
    21→  dueDate:   string    // 'YYYY-MM-DD' — ISO date, no time component
    22→  createdAt: number    // Unix ms, derived from Firestore serverTimestamp on read
    23→  updatedAt: number    // Unix ms
    24→}
    25→
    26→// What callers pass to addVideo — no auto-managed fields
    27→export type VideoInput = Omit<Video, 'id' | 'createdAt' | 'updatedAt'>
    28→
    29→// ── Derived helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    30→
    31→/**
    32→ * Returns true if the video's due date is strictly in the past
    33→ * (ignores time — a card due today is NOT overdue until tomorrow).
    34→ */
    35→export function isOverdue(video: Video): boolean {
    36→  if (!video.dueDate) return false
    37→  const today = new Date()
    38→  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0)
    39→  return new Date(video.dueDate) < today
    40→}
    41→

     1→import {
     2→  collection,
     3→  doc,
     4→  addDoc,
     5→  updateDoc,
     6→  deleteDoc,
     7→  onSnapshot,
     8→  query,
     9→  orderBy,
    10→  serverTimestamp,
    11→  Timestamp,
    12→} from 'firebase/firestore'
    13→import type { DocumentData, QueryDocumentSnapshot } from 'firebase/firestore'
    14→import { db } from './config'
    15→import type { Video, VideoInput } from '../types/video'
    16→
    17→const COL = collection(db, 'videos')
    18→
    19→// ── Firestore → app type conversion ──────────────────────────────────────────
    20→
    21→function fromDoc(snap: QueryDocumentSnapshot<DocumentData>): Video {
    22→  const d = snap.data()
    23→  return {
    24→    id:        snap.id,
    25→    title:     d.title     ?? '',
    26→    platform:  d.platform  ?? 'YouTube',
    27→    stage:     d.stage     ?? 'Idea',
    28→    creator:   d.creator   ?? 'Pab',
    29→    notes:     d.notes     ?? '',
    30→    dueDate:   d.dueDate   ?? '',
    31→    createdAt: (d.createdAt as Timestamp | null)?.toMillis() ?? Date.now(),
    32→    updatedAt: (d.updatedAt as Timestamp | null)?.toMillis() ?? Date.now(),
    33→  }
    34→}
    35→
    36→// ── Real-time subscription ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    37→
    38→/**
    39→ * Subscribes to the full videos collection, ordered by creation date.
    40→ * Both users see each other's changes in real time.
    41→ * Returns the unsubscribe function — call it in useEffect cleanup.
    42→ */
    43→export function subscribeToVideos(onChange: (videos: Video[]) => void): () => void {
    44→  const q = query(COL, orderBy('createdAt', 'desc'))
    45→  return onSnapshot(q, (snap) => {
    46→    onChange(snap.docs.map(fromDoc))
    47→  })
    48→}
    49→
    50→// ── CRUD ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    51→
    52→/**
    53→ * Creates a new video document.
    54→ * createdAt and updatedAt are set server-side.
    55→ */
    56→export async function addVideo(input: VideoInput): Promise<void> {
    57→  await addDoc(COL, {
    58→    ...input,
    59→    createdAt: serverTimestamp(),
    60→    updatedAt: serverTimestamp(),
    61→  })
    62→}
    63→
    64→/**
    65→ * Updates any subset of a video's fields.
    66→ * Used for both full edits and drag-drop stage changes:
    67→ *   updateVideo(id, { stage: 'Editing' })
    68→ */
    69→export async function updateVideo(id: string, changes: Partial<VideoInput>): Promise<void> {
    70→  await updateDoc(doc(COL, id), {
    71→    ...changes,
    72→    updatedAt: serverTimestamp(),
    73→  })
    74→}
    75→
    76→/**
    77→ * Permanently deletes a video document.
    78→ */
    79→export async function deleteVideo(id: string): Promise<void> {
    80→  await deleteDoc(doc(COL, id))
    81→}
    82→

     4→const PLATFORM_CLASS: Record<Platform, string> = {
     5→  'YouTube':  'platform-youtube',
     6→  'IG Reels': 'platform-ig',
     7→  'TikTok':   'platform-tiktok',
     8→}

    10→function formatDate(iso: string): string {
    11→  // 'YYYY-MM-DD' → 'MM/DD/YYYY'
    12→  const [y, m, d] = iso.split('-')
    13→  return `${m}/${d}/${y}`
    14→}
    15→
    16→interface Props {
    17→  video:  Video
    18→  onEdit: (video: Video) => void
    19→}
    20→
    21→export default function VideoCard({ video, onEdit }: Props) {
    22→  const overdue = isOverdue(video)
    23→
    24→  return (
    25→    <div
    26→      className={`video-card${overdue ? ' is-overdue' : ''}`}
    27→      draggable
    28→      onDragStart={(e) => {
    29→        e.dataTransfer.setData('videoId', video.id)
    30→        e.dataTransfer.setData('sourceStage', video.stage)
    31→        e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move'
    32→      }}
    33→    >
    34→      <div className="video-card-title">{video.title}</div>
    35→
    36→      <div className="video-card-meta">
    37→        <span className={`platform-badge ${PLATFORM_CLASS[video.platform]}`}>
    38→          {video.platform}
    39→        </span>
    40→        <span className="creator-tag">{video.creator}</span>
    41→        {overdue && <span className="overdue-badge">OVERDUE</span>}
    42→      </div>
    43→
    44→      {video.dueDate && (
    45→        <div className={`video-card-due${overdue ? ' overdue-text' : ''}`}>
    46→          DUE: {formatDate(video.dueDate)}
    47→        </div>
    48→      )}
    49→
    50→      {video.notes && (
    51→        <div className="video-card-notes">{video.notes}</div>
    52→      )}
    53→
    54→      <button className="video-card-edit-btn" onClick={() => onEdit(video)}>
    55→        EDIT
    56→      </button>
    57→    </div>
    58→  )
    59→}

Good. Here's what I see that needs to change:

**Type layer:** `Video` gets `titleOptions: TitleOption[]`. `VideoInput` needs to exclude it (the form doesn't manage title options). `VideoUpdate` replaces `Partial<VideoInput>` in `updateVideo` so it can accept `titleOptions` updates.

**Identity:** Both creators need to know "which one am I?" based on their logged-in email. Two new env vars (`VITE_PAB_EMAIL`, `VITE_OPHER_EMAIL`) + a `creatorFromEmail()` util solves it without building user profiles.

**Drag issue:** The card root is `draggable`. Clicking inside TitleTesting's input can accidentally trigger the drag gesture — I'll stop propagation inside that component.

Date.now(),\n    updatedAt:    (d.updatedAt as Timestamp | null)?.toMillis() ?? Date.now(),\n  }\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Real-time subscription \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Subscribes to the full videos collection, ordered by creation date.\n * Both users see each other's changes in real time.\n * Returns the unsubscribe function \u2014 call it in useEffect cleanup.\n */\nexport function subscribeToVideos(onChange: (videos: Video[]) => void): () => void {\n  const q = query(COL, orderBy('createdAt', 'desc'))\n  return onSnapshot(q, (snap) => {\n    onChange(snap.docs.map(fromDoc))\n  })\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 CRUD \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Creates a new video document.\n * titleOptions starts empty; createdAt/updatedAt are set server-side.\n */\nexport async function addVideo(input: VideoInput): Promise<void> {\n  await addDoc(COL, {\n    ...input,\n    titleOptions: [],\n    createdAt: serverTimestamp(),\n    updatedAt: serverTimestamp(),\n  })\n}\n\n/**\n * Updates any subset of a video's fields.\n * Handles full edits, drag-drop stage changes, and titleOptions updates:\n *   updateVideo(id, { stage: 'Editing' })\n *   updateVideo(id, { titleOptions: updatedArray })\n */\nexport async function updateVideo(id: string, changes: VideoUpdate): Promise<void> {\n  await updateDoc(doc(COL, id), {\n    ...changes,\n    updatedAt: serverTimestamp(),\n  })\n}\n\n/**\n * Permanently deletes a video document.\n */\nexport async function deleteVideo(id: string): Promise<void> {\n  await deleteDoc(doc(COL, id))\n}\n"
}

Title testing is done. Here's what was built and one setup step you need:

---

## What's live

Each card now has a **TITLE TEST [+]** toggle at the bottom. Click to expand:

```
TITLE TEST [+]  2                    ← count badge when options exist

"How We Grew 10k Subs in a Month"
                              [PAB]
                           ▲ 2  ▼ 0  ← your vote highlights (teal=up, coral=down)

"The Video That Changed Everything"
                            [OPHER]
                           ▲ 1  ▼ 1

┌─────────────────────────┐  [+]
│ Suggest a title...      │
└─────────────────────────┘
```

- Voting toggles — click the same direction again to clear your vote
- Both creators see each other's votes in real time via the Firestore subscription already running on the card
- The `draggable={false}` + `stopPropagation` on the section means clicking inside it won't accidentally drag the card

## One setup step
Add your real emails to `.env.local`:
```
VITE_PAB_EMAIL=pab-real-email@gmail.com
VITE_OPHER_EMAIL=opher-real-email@gmail.com
```
Vite requires a restart after `.env.local` changes. Without this, voting is disabled with an explanatory message — it degrades gracefully.

     1→import { useState } from 'react'
     2→import type { Stage, Video } from '../../types/video'
     3→import { updateVideo } from '../../firebase/videos'
     4→import VideoCard from './VideoCard'
     5→
     6→interface Props {
     7→  stage:      Stage
     8→  videos:     Video[]
     9→  onEditVideo: (video: Video) => void
    10→}
    11→
    12→export default function KanbanColumn({ stage, videos, onEditVideo }: Props) {
    13→  const [isDragOver, setIsDragOver] = useState(false)
    14→
    15→  async function handleDrop(e: React.DragEvent) {
    16→    e.preventDefault()
    17→    setIsDragOver(false)
    18→    const videoId     = e.dataTransfer.getData('videoId')
    19→    const sourceStage = e.dataTransfer.getData('sourceStage')
    20→    if (videoId && sourceStage !== stage) {
    21→      await updateVideo(videoId, { stage })
    22→    }
    23→  }
    24→
    25→  return (
    26→    <div className="kanban-column">
    27→      <div className="kanban-column-header">
    28→        <span>{stage.toUpperCase()}</span>
    29→        <span className="kanban-column-count">{videos.length}</span>
    30→      </div>
    31→
    32→      <div
    33→        className={`kanban-column-body${isDragOver ? ' drag-over' : ''}`}
    34→        onDragOver={(e) => e.preventDefault()}
    35→        onDragEnter={() => setIsDragOver(true)}
    36→        onDragLeave={(e) => {
    37→          // Only clear when actually leaving the column — not when entering a child card
    38→          const related = e.relatedTarget as Node | null
    39→          if (!related || !e.currentTarget.contains(related)) {
    40→            setIsDragOver(false)
    41→          }
    42→        }}
    43→        onDrop={handleDrop}
    44→      >
    45→        {videos.map((v) => (
    46→          <VideoCard key={v.id} video={v} onEdit={onEditVideo} />
    47→        ))}
    48→      </div>
    49→    </div>
    50→  )
    51→}
    52→

     1→import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
     2→import type { Video } from '../types/video'
     3→import { subscribeToVideos } from '../firebase/videos'
     4→import KanbanBoard from '../components/pipeline/KanbanBoard'
     5→import VideoForm   from '../components/pipeline/VideoForm'
     6→
     7→export default function Pipeline() {
     8→  const [videos,     setVideos]     = useState<Video[]>([])
     9→  const [editTarget, setEditTarget] = useState<Video | null>(null)
    10→  const [showAdd,    setShowAdd]    = useState(false)
    11→
    12→  useEffect(() => {
    13→    return subscribeToVideos(setVideos)
    14→  }, [])
    15→
    16→  const isFormOpen = showAdd || editTarget !== null
    17→
    18→  return (
    19→    <div className="pipeline-page">
    20→      <div className="pipeline-toolbar">
    21→        <h2 className="pipeline-heading">VIDEO PIPELINE</h2>
    22→        <button className="btn-primary" onClick={() => setShowAdd(true)}>
    23→          + ADD VIDEO
    24→        </button>
    25→      </div>
    26→
    27→      <KanbanBoard
    28→        videos={videos}
    29→        onEditVideo={setEditTarget}
    30→      />
    31→
    32→      {isFormOpen && (
    33→        <VideoForm
    34→          initial={editTarget}
    35→          onClose={() => { setShowAdd(false); setEditTarget(null) }}
    36→        />
    37→      )}
    38→    </div>
    39→  )
    40→}

--- CLAUDE ---
Clear picture. Here's the event chain:

- `VideoCard` puts `videoCreator` in `dataTransfer` (already has `videoId` + `sourceStage`)
- `KanbanColumn.handleDrop` detects when `stage === 'Published'`, calls `onVideoPublished()` callback + `recordPublish(creator)`
- `KanbanBoard` threads `onVideoPublished` through
- `Pipeline` owns confetti state + workspace subscription, renders the `<Confetti>` and streak display

For the streak: uses a `workspace/main` singleton document in Firestore. Uses a transaction so simultaneous publishes don't race. Streak only increments on Fridays — confetti fires for any publish regardless.

  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/firebase/workspace.ts",
  "content": "import { doc, onSnapshot, runTransaction } from 'firebase/firestore'\nimport { db } from './config'\nimport type { Creator } from '../types/video'\nimport type { Workspace } from '../types/workspace'\nimport { WORKSPACE_DEFAULTS } from '../types/workspace'\n\nconst WORKSPACE_REF = doc(db, 'workspace', 'main')\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Date helpers \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/** Returns local date as 'YYYY-MM-DD', avoiding UTC offset issues. */\nfunction localDateString(date: Date): string {\n  const y = date.getFullYear()\n  const m = String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')\n  const d = String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')\n  return `${y}-${m}-${d}`\n}\n\n/**\n * If today is Friday, returns today's date string.\n * Otherwise returns null \u2014 streak only counts on Fridays.\n */\nfunction todayIfFriday(): string | null {\n  const now = new Date()\n  return now.getDay() === 5 ? localDateString(now) : null\n}\n\n/** Returns the date of the Friday exactly one week before the given Friday. */\nfunction prevFriday(friday: string): string {\n  const d = new Date(friday + 'T12:00:00') // noon avoids DST edge cases\n  d.setDate(d.getDate() - 7)\n  return localDateString(d)\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Subscription \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport function subscribeToWorkspace(onChange: (ws: Workspace) => void): () => void {\n  return onSnapshot(WORKSPACE_REF, (snap) => {\n    if (snap.exists()) {\n      onChange(snap.data() as Workspace)\n    } else {\n      onChange(WORKSPACE_DEFAULTS)\n    }\n  })\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Streak logic \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Called whenever a video card is moved to Published.\n * Confetti always fires (handled by caller).\n * Streak only advances if today is a Friday and both creators publish on the same Friday.\n */\nexport async function recordPublish(creator: Creator): Promise<void> {\n  const friday = todayIfFriday()\n  if (!friday) return // Not a Friday \u2014 confetti still fires, streak unchanged\n\n  await runTransaction(db, async (tx) => {\n    const snap    = await tx.get(WORKSPACE_REF)\n    const current = snap.exists() ? (snap.data() as Workspace) : { ...WORKSPACE_DEFAULTS }\n\n    // If this is a new Friday, reset the per-week tracker\n    const isNewWeek = current.thisWeekFriday !== friday\n    const thisWeek  = isNewWeek\n      ? { Pab: false, Opher: false }\n      : { ...current.thisWeekPublished }\n\n    // Record this creator as published this Friday\n    thisWeek[creator] = true\n\n    let { streakCount, lastStreakFriday } = current\n\n    // If both published this Friday and we haven't already counted this Friday\n    if (thisWeek.Pab && thisWeek.Opher && lastStreakFriday !== friday) {\n      const wasConsecutive = lastStreakFriday === prevFriday(friday)\n      streakCount      = wasConsecutive ? streakCount + 1 : 1\n      lastStreakFriday = friday\n    }\n\n    tx.set(WORKSPACE_REF, {\n      streakCount,\n      lastStreakFriday,\n      thisWeekFriday:    friday,\n      thisWeekPublished: thisWeek,\n    })\n  })\n}\n"
}

--- CLAUDE ---
Feature 2 is done. Here's the full picture:

---

## What's live

**Confetti** — any time you drag a card into the Published column, 55 colored squares rain down the screen for ~3 seconds. Uses the exact same color palette as the sparkle trail already in the app so it feels intentional, not bolted-on.

**Streak counter** — lives in the pipeline toolbar:

```
>> VIDEO PIPELINE          STREAK  3  FRIDAYS    [+ ADD VIDEO]
```

**Streak logic:**

| Scenario | Result |
|---|---|
| Card dropped to Published, not a Friday | Confetti fires, streak unchanged |
| Card dropped to Published on a Friday, only one creator published today | Confetti fires, streak unchanged |
| Both creators publish on the same Friday, last streak Friday was 7 days ago | Streak++ |
| Both publish on the same Friday, but last streak Friday was 2+ weeks ago | Streak resets to 1 |
| Both publish on the same Friday again in same week | No double-count (idempotent) |

The write uses a Firestore **transaction** — if both of you drag cards to Published within milliseconds of each other, only one wins the increment and the count stays correct.

**One step required:** Paste the updated `firestore.rules` into Firebase Console → Firestore → Rules. The `workspace` collection is new and won't be writable until that rule is added.

---

Ready for feature 3 (live URL field on Published cards) whenever you say go.

[tool_use: Write]
{
  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/firebase/workspace.ts",
  "content": "import { doc, onSnapshot, runTransaction } from 'firebase/firestore'\nimport { db } from './config'\nimport type { Creator } from '../types/video'\nimport type { Workspace } from '../types/workspace'\nimport { WORKSPACE_DEFAULTS } from '../types/workspace'\n\nconst WORKSPACE_REF = doc(db, 'workspace', 'main')\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Date helpers \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/** Local date as 'YYYY-MM-DD' \u2014 avoids UTC offset shifting the date. */\nfunction localDateString(date: Date): string {\n  const y = date.getFullYear()\n  const m = String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')\n  const d = String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')\n  return `${y}-${m}-${d}`\n}\n\n/**\n * Returns the Monday of the ISO week containing the given date (local time).\n * Sunday is treated as the last day of the previous week.\n */\nfunction getWeekStart(date: Date): string {\n  const d   = new Date(date)\n  const day = d.getDay()                  // 0=Sun, 1=Mon \u2026 6=Sat\n  const diff = day === 0 ? -6 : 1 - day  // shift back to Monday\n  d.setDate(d.getDate() + diff)\n  return localDateString(d)\n}\n\n/** Returns the Monday of the week before the given week-start date. */\nfunction prevWeekStart(weekStart: string): string {\n  const d = new Date(weekStart + 'T12:00:00') // noon avoids DST edge cases\n  d.setDate(d.getDate() - 7)\n  return localDateString(d)\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Subscription \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport function subscribeToWorkspace(onChange: (ws: Workspace) => void): () => void {\n  return onSnapshot(WORKSPACE_REF, (snap) => {\n    onChange(snap.exists() ? (snap.data() as Workspace) : { ...WORKSPACE_DEFAULTS })\n  })\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 Streak logic \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Records a publish for one creator.\n * - Each creator has their own independent streak.\n * - Streak tracks consecutive calendar weeks (Mon\u2013Sun), any day of the week.\n * - Calling this multiple times in the same week is idempotent.\n * - Confetti is always triggered by the caller regardless of streak changes.\n */\nexport async function recordPublish(creator: Creator): Promise<void> {\n  const weekStart = getWeekStart(new Date())\n\n  await runTransaction(db, async (tx) => {\n    const snap    = await tx.get(WORKSPACE_REF)\n    const current: Workspace = snap.exists()\n      ? (snap.data() as Workspace)\n      : { ...WORKSPACE_DEFAULTS }\n\n    const existing = current.streaks?.[creator] ?? { count: 0, lastWeekStart: null }\n\n    // Already published this week \u2014 no change needed\n    if (existing.lastWeekStart === weekStart) return\n\n    const wasConsecutive = existing.lastWeekStart === prevWeekStart(weekStart)\n\n    tx.set(WORKSPACE_REF, {\n      ...current,\n      streaks: {\n        ...current.streaks,\n        [creator]: {\n          count:         wasConsecutive ? existing.count + 1 : 1,\n          lastWeekStart: weekStart,\n        },\n      },\n    })\n  })\n}\n"
}

--- CLAUDE ---
Done. Here's what changed and why:

---

## Streaks — redesigned

**Before:** one shared streak, Friday-only, both creators had to publish on the same day.

**Now:** each creator has their own independent streak, tracked by calendar week (Monday–Sunday), any day of the week.

```
>> VIDEO PIPELINE     [PAB  5 WKS]  [OPHER  3 WKS]   [+ ADD VIDEO]
```

| Scenario | Result |
|---|---|
| Pab publishes twice in week 11 | Streak only increments once (idempotent) |
| Pab published week 10 + week 11 | Streak++ |
| Pab skipped week 10 | Streak resets to 1 |
| Opher's streak is completely independent | Always |

The `workspace/main` document now looks like: `{ streaks: { Pab: { count: 5, lastWeekStart: "2026-03-09" }, Opher: { count: 3, lastWeekStart: "2026-03-09" } } }`.

---

## Responsive — what changes at each breakpoint

**Mobile (≤767px):**
- Sidebar hidden → `[=]` hamburger appears in header, click drops nav inline below header, click a link closes it
- Email address hidden from header (too long for small screens)
- Content padding drops from `2rem` → `1rem`
- Pipeline toolbar and streak badges wrap naturally
- Kanban columns narrow to 200px, horizontal scroll works via `min-width: 0` on flex children
- Modal slides up from the bottom edge instead of centering
- Login box tightens padding

**Tablet (768–1023px):**
- Sidebar stays but narrows to 170px
- Kanban columns at 200px

**Desktop (≥1024px):**
- Unchanged from before

--- YOU ---
Add a global creator filter to the app. It should live in the header or sidebar and have three options: All, Pab, and Opher. When a creator is selected it filters everything across the entire app, the pipeline board, stats, performance cards, everything. Store the active filter in React Context so any page can read it without prop drilling. No new Firestore reads needed, just filter already loaded data based on the creator tag. Maybe have a color cue.

Clear plan:

- `FilterContext` wraps the whole app alongside `AuthProvider` — `FilterCreator = 'All' | 'Pab' | 'Opher'`
- `CreatorFilter` is a reusable component dropped into both the sidebar (desktop) and the mobile nav dropdown — one source of truth for the UI
- Colors: **All** = yellow, **Pab** = coral, **Opher** = teal — these same colors appear on the `creator-tag` of every video card, so the filter and the cards share a visual language
- Pipeline filters `videos` before passing to `KanbanBoard` — zero extra reads

  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/context/FilterContext.tsx",
  "content": "import { createContext, useContext, useState } from 'react'\nimport type { ReactNode } from 'react'\nimport type { Creator } from '../types/video'\n\nexport type FilterCreator = Creator | 'All'\n\ninterface FilterContextValue {\n  activeCreator:    FilterCreator\n  setActiveCreator: (c: FilterCreator) => void\n}\n\nconst FilterContext = createContext<FilterContextValue>({\n  activeCreator:    'All',\n  setActiveCreator: () => {},\n})\n\nexport function FilterProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {\n  const [activeCreator, setActiveCreator] = useState<FilterCreator>('All')\n\n  return (\n    <FilterContext.Provider value={{ activeCreator, setActiveCreator }}>\n      {children}\n    </FilterContext.Provider>\n  )\n}\n\nexport function useFilter() {\n  return useContext(FilterContext)\n}\n"
}

--- CLAUDE ---
Done. Here's exactly what was built and how the color system ties together:

---

## What's live

**Sidebar (desktop) — pinned to the bottom:**
```
# DASHBOARD
> VIDEO PIPELINE


  ─────────────────
  FILTER
  [ ALL ] [ PAB ] [ OPHER ]
```

**Mobile nav — appears below nav links when `[=]` is tapped:**
```
# DASHBOARD
> VIDEO PIPELINE
─────────────────
  FILTER
  [ ALL ] [ PAB ] [ OPHER ]
```

**Active state colors:**

| Selection | Button | Creator tag on cards |
|---|---|---|
| ALL | yellow border + bg tint | Pab=coral, Opher=teal |
| PAB | coral fill | all visible cards = coral |
| OPHER | teal fill | all visible cards = teal |

The filter button color and the `creator-tag` badge color are the same accent color for each creator — so when you select PAB, the filter button turns coral AND every card in the board has a coral [PAB] tag. The visual language is consistent end-to-end.

**How new pages tap into the filter** — zero prop drilling, one import:
```ts
const { activeCreator } = useFilter()
const filtered = activeCreator === 'All' ? data : data.filter(d => d.creator === activeCreator)
```

     2→import type { Video } from '../types/video'
     3→import type { Workspace } from '../types/workspace'
     4→import { subscribeToVideos } from '../firebase/videos'
     5→import { subscribeToWorkspace } from '../firebase/workspace'
     6→import { useFilter } from '../context/FilterContext'
     7→import KanbanBoard from '../components/pipeline/KanbanBoard'
     8→import VideoForm   from '../components/pipeline/VideoForm'
     9→import Confetti    from '../components/Confetti'
    10→
    11→export default function Pipeline() {
    12→  const [videos,       setVideos]       = useState<Video[]>([])
    13→  const [workspace,    setWorkspace]    = useState<Workspace | null>(null)
    14→  const [editTarget,   setEditTarget]   = useState<Video | null>(null)
    15→  const [showAdd,      setShowAdd]      = useState(false)
    16→  const [showConfetti, setShowConfetti] = useState(false)
    17→
    18→  useEffect(() => subscribeToVideos(setVideos),       [])
    19→  useEffect(() => subscribeToWorkspace(setWorkspace), [])
    20→
    21→  const { activeCreator } = useFilter()
    22→
    23→  const isFormOpen  = showAdd || editTarget !== null
    24→  const pabStreak   = workspace?.streaks?.Pab?.count   ?? 0
    25→  const opherStreak = workspace?.streaks?.Opher?.count ?? 0
    26→
    27→  const filteredVideos = activeCreator === 'All'
    28→    ? videos
    29→    : videos.filter((v) => v.creator === activeCreator)
    30→
    31→  return (
    32→    <div className="pipeline-page">
    33→      <div className="pipeline-toolbar">
    34→        <h2 className="pipeline-heading">VIDEO PIPELINE</h2>
    35→        <div className="pipeline-toolbar-right">
    36→          <div className="streak-badge">
    37→            <span className="streak-name">PAB</span>
    38→            <span className="streak-number">{pabStreak}</span>
    39→            <span className="streak-unit">{pabStreak === 1 ? 'WK' : 'WKS'}</span>
    40→          </div>
    41→          <div className="streak-badge">
    42→            <span className="streak-name">OPHER</span>
    43→            <span className="streak-number">{opherStreak}</span>
    44→            <span className="streak-unit">{opherStreak === 1 ? 'WK' : 'WKS'}</span>
    45→          </div>
    46→          <button className="btn-primary" onClick={() => setShowAdd(true)}>
    47→            + ADD VIDEO
    48→          </button>
    49→        </div>
    50→      </div>
    51→
    52→      <KanbanBoard
    53→        videos={filteredVideos}
    54→        onEditVideo={setEditTarget}
    55→        onVideoPublished={() => setShowConfetti(true)}
    56→      />
    57→
    58→      {isFormOpen && (
    59→        <VideoForm
    60→          initial={editTarget}
    61→          onClose={() => { setShowAdd(false); setEditTarget(null) }}
    62→        />
    63→      )}
    64→

    67→  )

  "content": "import { PLATFORMS, STAGES } from '../../types/video'\nimport type { Platform, Stage } from '../../types/video'\n\ninterface Props {\n  search:     string\n  platform:   Platform | ''\n  stage:      Stage | ''\n  onSearch:   (v: string) => void\n  onPlatform: (v: Platform | '') => void\n  onStage:    (v: Stage | '') => void\n}\n\nexport default function PipelineFilters({\n  search, platform, stage,\n  onSearch, onPlatform, onStage,\n}: Props) {\n  const hasFilters = search !== '' || platform !== '' || stage !== ''\n\n  function clearAll() {\n    onSearch('')\n    onPlatform('')\n    onStage('')\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"pipeline-filters\">\n      <input\n        className=\"filter-search\"\n        type=\"text\"\n        value={search}\n        onChange={(e) => onSearch(e.target.value)}\n        placeholder=\"SEARCH TITLES...\"\n        spellCheck={false}\n      />\n\n      <select\n        className=\"filter-select\"\n        value={platform}\n        onChange={(e) => onPlatform(e.target.value as Platform | '')}\n      >\n        <option value=\"\">ALL PLATFORMS</option>\n        {PLATFORMS.map((p) => (\n          <option key={p} value={p}>{p}</option>\n        ))}\n      </select>\n\n      <select\n        className=\"filter-select\"\n        value={stage}\n        onChange={(e) => onStage(e.target.value as Stage | '')}\n      >\n        <option value=\"\">ALL STAGES</option>\n        {STAGES.map((s) => (\n          <option key={s} value={s}>{s.toUpperCase()}</option>\n        ))}\n      </select>\n\n      {hasFilters && (\n        <button className=\"filter-clear-btn\" onClick={clearAll}>\n          CLEAR [X]\n        </button>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"
}

  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/pages/Pipeline.tsx",
  "content": "import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react'\nimport type { Platform, Stage, Video } from '../types/video'\nimport type { Workspace } from '../types/workspace'\nimport { subscribeToVideos } from '../firebase/videos'\nimport { subscribeToWorkspace } from '../firebase/workspace'\nimport { useFilter } from '../context/FilterContext'\nimport KanbanBoard     from '../components/pipeline/KanbanBoard'\nimport VideoForm       from '../components/pipeline/VideoForm'\nimport PipelineFilters from '../components/pipeline/PipelineFilters'\nimport Confetti        from '../components/Confetti'\n\nexport default function Pipeline() {\n  const [videos,       setVideos]       = useState<Video[]>([])\n  const [workspace,    setWorkspace]    = useState<Workspace | null>(null)\n  const [editTarget,   setEditTarget]   = useState<Video | null>(null)\n  const [showAdd,      setShowAdd]      = useState(false)\n  const [showConfetti, setShowConfetti] = useState(false)\n\n  // Search / filter bar state\n  const [search,          setSearch]          = useState('')\n  const [filterPlatform,  setFilterPlatform]  = useState<Platform | ''>('')\n  const [filterStage,     setFilterStage]     = useState<Stage | ''>('')\n\n  useEffect(() => subscribeToVideos(setVideos),       [])\n  useEffect(() => subscribeToWorkspace(setWorkspace), [])\n\n  const { activeCreator } = useFilter()\n\n  const pabStreak   = workspace?.streaks?.Pab?.count   ?? 0\n  const opherStreak = workspace?.streaks?.Opher?.count ?? 0\n\n  // All filters applied in sequence \u2014 no extra Firestore reads\n  const filteredVideos = useMemo(() => {\n    let result = videos\n\n    // Global creator filter (from sidebar/nav)\n    if (activeCreator !== 'All') {\n      result = result.filter((v) => v.creator === activeCreator)\n    }\n    // Title search\n    if (search.trim()) {\n      const q = search.trim().toLowerCase()\n      result = result.filter((v) => v.title.toLowerCase().includes(q))\n    }\n    // Platform dropdown\n    if (filterPlatform) {\n      result = result.filter((v) => v.platform === filterPlatform)\n    }\n    // Stage dropdown\n    if (filterStage) {\n      result = result.filter((v) => v.stage === filterStage)\n    }\n\n    return result\n  }, [videos, activeCreator, search, filterPlatform, filterStage])\n\n  const isFormOpen = showAdd || editTarget !== null\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"pipeline-page\">\n      <div className=\"pipeline-toolbar\">\n        <h2 className=\"pipeline-heading\">VIDEO PIPELINE</h2>\n        <div className=\"pipeline-toolbar-right\">\n          <div className=\"streak-badge\">\n            <span className=\"streak-name\">PAB</span>\n            <span className=\"streak-number\">{pabStreak}</span>\n            <span className=\"streak-unit\">{pabStreak === 1 ? 'WK' : 'WKS'}</span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"streak-badge\">\n            <span className=\"streak-name\">OPHER</span>\n            <span className=\"streak-number\">{opherStreak}</span>\n            <span className=\"streak-unit\">{opherStreak === 1 ? 'WK' : 'WKS'}</span>\n          </div>\n          <button className=\"btn-primary\" onClick={() => setShowAdd(true)}>\n            + ADD VIDEO\n          </button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      <PipelineFilters\n        search={search}\n        platform={filterPlatform}\n        stage={filterStage}\n        onSearch={setSearch}\n        onPlatform={setFilterPlatform}\n        onStage={setFilterStage}\n      />\n\n      <KanbanBoard\n        videos={filteredVideos}\n        onEditVideo={setEditTarget}\n        onVideoPublished={() => setShowConfetti(true)}\n      />\n\n      {isFormOpen && (\n        <VideoForm\n          initial={editTarget}\n          onClose={() => { setShowAdd(false); setEditTarget(null) }}\n        />\n      )}\n\n      {showConfetti && <Confetti onDone={() => setShowConfetti(false)} />}\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n"
}

--- CLAUDE ---
Done. Here's everything:

---

## Filter bar — above the kanban columns

```
[ SEARCH TITLES...          ]  [ ALL PLATFORMS ▼ ]  [ ALL STAGES ▼ ]  CLEAR [X]
```

All three filters compose — selecting "YouTube" + "Editing" shows only YouTube cards in the Editing column. The global creator filter from the sidebar stacks on top of all three. `CLEAR [X]` only appears when at least one filter is active.

**On mobile:** search input goes full-width on its own row, the two dropdowns share the row below it.

**Filter priority chain:**
```
All videos
  → creator filter (context)
    → text search (title contains)
      → platform dropdown
        → stage dropdown
```

---

## Seed data — 13 mock videos

Go to `/app/dashboard`, click **[DEV] SEED SAMPLE DATA**, confirm. It inserts 13 videos across all 5 stages, both creators, all 3 platforms — including 2 with past due dates that will show as `OVERDUE`.

The button only renders when `import.meta.env.DEV === true` — it will never appear in your Netlify production build. Once you have real data, delete the cards via the pipeline board and remove the seed button from `Dashboard.tsx`.

--- YOU ---
Add YouTube Data API integration to the Channel Stats page. I need to pull real stats for our channel using the YouTube Data API v3. Set up OAuth 2.0 so each creator authenticates with their own Google account and we can pull their individual video stats. For each published video that has a live URL in Firestore, fetch the real view count, like count, and comment count from the API and display them on the performance card. Store the API key in .env.local as VITE_YOUTUBE_API_KEY. Walk me through the Google Cloud Console setup first before writing any code.

--- CLAUDE ---


--- CLAUDE ---
Before writing any code, I need to flag two things that will affect how we set this up:

---

## Architecture clarification first

**OAuth 2.0 is not needed for your stated goal.**

View count, like count, and comment count on published videos are **public data**. The YouTube Data API v3 `videos.list` endpoint returns these stats using just an API key — no OAuth, no user login. OAuth is only required for private analytics data like impressions, click-through rate, subscriber change, and revenue (that's the separate YouTube Analytics API).

If you want those private metrics eventually, OAuth is the right path. But for the three fields you described, an API key is sufficient and the implementation is dramatically simpler.

**`VITE_YOUTUBE_API_KEY` would be a security problem.**

Any environment variable prefixed `VITE_` in a Vite app gets **compiled directly into the JavaScript bundle** that ships to the browser. Anyone who opens DevTools → Sources can read it. For a YouTube API key, that means someone can extract it and burn through your quota.

The correct pattern is:
```
Browser → Netlify Function (serverless) → YouTube API (key lives server-side)
```

The API key lives in a **Netlify environment variable** (no `VITE_` prefix, never touches the client bundle). A thin Netlify Function proxies the request. Since you're already on Netlify, this costs nothing and adds no new infrastructure.

---

## Google Cloud Console setup walkthrough

### Step 1 — Create a project

1. Go to [console.cloud.google.com](https://console.cloud.google.com)
2. Click the project dropdown at the top → **New Project**
3. Name it `pabopher-dashboard` → Create
4. Make sure that project is selected in the dropdown before continuing

---

### Step 2 — Enable the YouTube Data API v3

1. Left sidebar → **APIs & Services** → **Library**
2. Search `YouTube Data API v3`
3. Click it → **Enable**
4. Wait for it to activate (takes ~10 seconds)

---

### Step 3 — Create an API key

1. Left sidebar → **APIs & Services** → **Credentials**
2. **+ Create Credentials** → **API key**
3. A key is generated — copy it immediately, you'll paste it into Netlify
4. Click **Edit API key** (pencil icon) to restrict it:

**Application restrictions:**
- Select **HTTP referrers (websites)**
- Add your Netlify domain: `https://your-app.netlify.app/*`
- Also add `http://localhost:5173/*` for local development

**API restrictions:**
- Select **Restrict key**
- Choose **YouTube Data API v3** from the list

5. Save

This means even if someone extracts the key from a network request, it only works from your domain and only against YouTube's API.

---

### Step 4 — Add the key to Netlify (not `.env.local`)

In the Netlify dashboard:
1. Site → **Site configuration** → **Environment variables**
2. Add variable: `YOUTUBE_API_KEY` = your key (no `VITE_` prefix)
3. Scopes: all (or just Functions)

For **local development**, add it to `.env.local` as `YOUTUBE_API_KEY` (still no `VITE_` prefix) — Netlify Dev reads this for local function execution.

Update `.env.local.example`:
```
# YouTube Data API — server-side only, NOT VITE_ prefixed
# Used by Netlify Functions, never exposed to the browser
YOUTUBE_API_KEY=
```

---

### Step 5 — Netlify Functions setup

You'll need the Netlify CLI for local dev:
```bash
npm install -D netlify-cli @netlify/functions
```

Create `netlify.toml` in the project root:
```toml
[build]
  command   = "npm run build"
  publish   = "dist"
  functions = "netlify/functions"

[dev]
  command = "npm run dev"
  port    = 8888
```

Local dev changes: instead of `npm run dev`, you run `netlify dev` — it spins up both Vite and the Functions runtime on port 8888.

---

### What the function will do

The Netlify Function receives a YouTube video ID, calls `videos.list?part=statistics&id={videoId}&key={YOUTUBE_API_KEY}`, and returns `{ viewCount, likeCount, commentCount }`. The client never sees the key.

The video ID gets parsed from the live URL already stored in Firestore:
- `https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dQw4w9WgXcQ` → `dQw4w9WgXcQ`
- `https://youtu.be/dQw4w9WgXcQ` → `dQw4w9WgXcQ`

---

### If you want OAuth later (private analytics)

Come back to Cloud Console and:
1. **APIs & Services → OAuth consent screen** — fill in app name, support email, add scope `https://www.googleapis.com/auth/yt-analytics.readonly`, add both creator emails as test users
2. **Credentials → Create OAuth 2.0 Client ID** — Web application type, add your redirect URIs
3. Enable the **YouTube Analytics API** (separate from Data API v3)

This is a larger build — involves token storage in Firestore, refresh token handling, and a per-user auth flow. Worth doing once the basic stats are working.

---

    45→export type VideoUpdate = Partial<Omit<Video, 'id' | 'createdAt'>>
    46→

    48→
    49→/**
    50→ * Returns true if the video's due date is strictly in the past
    51→ * (ignores time — a card due today is NOT overdue until tomorrow).
    52→ */
    53→export function isOverdue(video: Video): boolean {
    54→  if (!video.dueDate) return false
    55→  const today = new Date()
    56→  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0)
    57→  return new Date(video.dueDate) < today
    58→}
    59→
    60→/** Up and down vote totals for a single title option. */
    61→export function countVotes(option: TitleOption): { up: number; down: number } {
    62→  const vals = Object.values(option.votes)
    63→  return {
    64→    up:   vals.filter((v) => v === 'up').length,
    65→    down: vals.filter((v) => v === 'down').length,
    66→  }
    67→}

     export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
       const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null)
       const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
       useEffect(() => {
         const unsub = onAuthStateChanged(auth, (u) => { setUser(u); setLoading(false) })
         return unsub
       }, [])
       return <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, loading }}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>
     }
     ```

       return <FilterContext.Provider value={{ activeCreator, setActiveCreator }}>{children}</FilterContext.Provider>

     export async function recordPublish(creator: Creator): Promise<void> {
       const weekStart = getWeekStart(new Date())
       await runTransaction(db, async (tx) => {
         const existing = current.streaks?.[creator] ?? { count: 0, lastWeekStart: null }
         if (existing.lastWeekStart === weekStart) return  // idempotent
         const wasConsecutive = existing.lastWeekStart === prevWeekStart(weekStart)
         tx.set(WORKSPACE_REF, { ...current, streaks: { ...current.streaks,
           [creator]: { count: wasConsecutive ? existing.count + 1 : 1, lastWeekStart: weekStart }
         }})
       })
     }
     ```

     export function creatorFromEmail(email: string | null | undefined): Creator | null {
       if (email === import.meta.env.VITE_PAB_EMAIL) return 'Pab'
       if (email === import.meta.env.VITE_OPHER_EMAIL) return 'Opher'
       return null
     }
