4. Errors and fixes:
   - No runtime errors encountered. All changes were written and verified via file structure checks.
   - One architectural correction: user requested streak redesign — original was a shared Friday-only streak; redesigned to two independent per-creator weekly streaks tracking consecutive calendar weeks (Mon–Sun) with no day-of-week restriction.

5. Problem Solving:
   - **Creator identity without user profiles**: Solved using VITE_PAB_EMAIL / VITE_OPHER_EMAIL env vars + creatorFromEmail() utility, avoiding the need to build a full user profile system
   - **Drag-and-drop + interactive children**: TitleTesting uses `onDragStart={e => e.stopPropagation()} draggable={false}` to prevent accidental drags when clicking inside title options
   - **Streak race condition**: Using Firestore `runTransaction` so simultaneous publishes don't double-count
   - **`min-width: 0` on flex children**: Critical fix for kanban horizontal scroll — without it, flex children blow out the layout on mobile
   - **VITE_ key exposure**: Correctly identified that VITE_YOUTUBE_API_KEY would be bundled into client JS; redirected to Netlify Functions proxy pattern with server-side key
   - **OAuth vs API key clarification**: Public YouTube stats (views/likes/comments) don't require OAuth — API key only; OAuth is only needed for private YouTube Analytics data
   - **`onDragLeave` flickering**: Fixed using `contains(relatedTarget)` check so drag-over state doesn't flicker when moving cursor over child elements within the column

     2→

     4→export type Stage    = 'Idea' | 'Scripting' | 'Filming' | 'Editing' | 'Published'
     5→export type Creator  = 'Pab' | 'Opher'
     6→
     7→// Ordered — used to render columns left-to-right
     8→export const STAGES: Stage[]       = ['Idea', 'Scripting', 'Filming', 'Editing', 'Published']
     9→export const PLATFORMS: Platform[] = ['YouTube', 'IG Reels', 'TikTok']
    10→export const CREATORS: Creator[]   = ['Pab', 'Opher']
    11→
    12→// ── Title testing ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    13→
    14→export interface TitleOptionVotes {
    15→  Pab:   'up' | 'down' | null
    16→  Opher: 'up' | 'down' | null
    17→}
    18→
    19→export interface TitleOption {
    20→  id:          string       // crypto.randomUUID()
    21→  text:        string
    22→  submittedBy: Creator
    23→  votes:       TitleOptionVotes
    24→}
    25→
    26→// ── Core model ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    27→
    28→export interface Video {
    29→  id:           string    // Firestore document ID
    30→  title:        string
    31→  platform:     Platform
    32→  stage:        Stage
    33→  creator:      Creator
    34→  notes:        string
    35→  dueDate:      string    // 'YYYY-MM-DD'
    36→  titleOptions: TitleOption[]
    37→  createdAt:    number    // Unix ms
    38→  updatedAt:    number    // Unix ms
    39→}
    40→
    41→// What VideoForm passes to addVideo — titleOptions are managed separately
    42→export type VideoInput = Omit<Video, 'id' | 'createdAt' | 'updatedAt' | 'titleOptions'>
    43→
    44→// Broader partial used by updateVideo — covers titleOptions, stage changes, etc.
    45→export type VideoUpdate = Partial<Omit<Video, 'id' | 'createdAt'>>
    46→
    47→// ── Derived helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    48→
    49→/**
    50→ * Returns true if the video's due date is strictly in the past
    51→ * (ignores time — a card due today is NOT overdue until tomorrow).
    52→ */
    53→export function isOverdue(video: Video): boolean {
    54→  if (!video.dueDate) return false
    55→  const today = new Date()
    56→  today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0)
    57→  return new Date(video.dueDate) < today
    58→}
    59→
    60→/** Up and down vote totals for a single title option. */
    61→export function countVotes(option: TitleOption): { up: number; down: number } {
    62→  const vals = Object.values(option.votes)
    63→  return {
    64→    up:   vals.filter((v) => v === 'up').length,
    65→    down: vals.filter((v) => v === 'down').length,
    66→  }
    67→}

     1→import {
     2→  collection,
     3→  doc,
     4→  addDoc,
     5→  updateDoc,
     6→  deleteDoc,
     7→  onSnapshot,
     8→  query,
     9→  orderBy,
    10→  serverTimestamp,
    11→  Timestamp,
    12→} from 'firebase/firestore'
    13→import type { DocumentData, QueryDocumentSnapshot } from 'firebase/firestore'
    14→import { db } from './config'
    15→import type { Video, VideoInput, VideoUpdate } from '../types/video'
    16→
    17→const COL = collection(db, 'videos')
    18→
    19→// ── Firestore → app type conversion ──────────────────────────────────────────
    20→
    21→function fromDoc(snap: QueryDocumentSnapshot<DocumentData>): Video {
    22→  const d = snap.data()
    23→  return {
    24→    id:           snap.id,
    25→    title:        d.title        ?? '',
    26→    platform:     d.platform     ?? 'YouTube',
    27→    stage:        d.stage        ?? 'Idea',
    28→    creator:      d.creator      ?? 'Pab',
    29→    notes:        d.notes        ?? '',
    30→    dueDate:      d.dueDate      ?? '',
    31→    titleOptions: d.titleOptions ?? [],
    32→    createdAt:    (d.createdAt as Timestamp | null)?.toMillis() ?? Date.now(),
    33→    updatedAt:    (d.updatedAt as Timestamp | null)?.toMillis() ?? Date.now(),
    34→  }
    35→}
    36→
    37→// ── Real-time subscription ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    38→
    39→/**
    40→ * Subscribes to the full videos collection, ordered by creation date.
    41→ * Both users see each other's changes in real time.
    42→ * Returns the unsubscribe function — call it in useEffect cleanup.
    43→ */
    44→export function subscribeToVideos(onChange: (videos: Video[]) => void): () => void {
    45→  const q = query(COL, orderBy('createdAt', 'desc'))
    46→  return onSnapshot(q, (snap) => {
    47→    onChange(snap.docs.map(fromDoc))
    48→  })
    49→}
    50→
    51→// ── CRUD ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    52→
    53→/**
    54→ * Creates a new video document.
    55→ * titleOptions starts empty; createdAt/updatedAt are set server-side.
    56→ */
    57→export async function addVideo(input: VideoInput): Promise<void> {
    58→  await addDoc(COL, {
    59→    ...input,
    60→    titleOptions: [],
    61→    createdAt: serverTimestamp(),
    62→    updatedAt: serverTimestamp(),
    63→  })
    64→}
    65→
    66→/**
    67→ * Updates any subset of a video's fields.
    68→ * Handles full edits, drag-drop stage changes, and titleOptions updates:
    69→ *   updateVideo(id, { stage: 'Editing' })
    70→ *   updateVideo(id, { titleOptions: updatedArray })
    71→ */
    72→export async function updateVideo(id: string, changes: VideoUpdate): Promise<void> {
    73→  await updateDoc(doc(COL, id), {
    74→    ...changes,
    75→    updatedAt: serverTimestamp(),
    76→  })
    77→}
    78→
    79→/**
    80→ * Permanently deletes a video document.
    81→ */
    82→export async function deleteVideo(id: string): Promise<void> {
    83→  await deleteDoc(doc(COL, id))
    84→}
    85→

    37→  function set<K extends keyof VideoInput>(key: K, value: VideoInput[K]) {
    38→    setFields((prev) => ({ ...prev, [key]: value }))
    39→  }

    41→  async function handleSubmit(e: FormEvent) {

    45→    setError('')

    48→        await updateVideo(initial.id, fields)
    49→      } else {
    50→        await addVideo(fields)
    51→      }
    52→      onClose()
    53→    } catch (err) {
    54→      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Something went wrong.')
    55→      setBusy(false)
    56→    }
    57→  }
    58→
    59→  async function handleDelete() {

    64→      await deleteVideo(initial.id)

  "content": "import type { Handler, HandlerEvent } from '@netlify/functions'\n\nconst YT_API = 'https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos'\n\nexport const handler: Handler = async (event: HandlerEvent) => {\n  const videoId = event.queryStringParameters?.videoId\n\n  if (!videoId) {\n    return { statusCode: 400, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Missing videoId' }) }\n  }\n\n  const apiKey = process.env.YOUTUBE_API_KEY\n  if (!apiKey) {\n    return { statusCode: 500, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'API key not configured' }) }\n  }\n\n  const url = `${YT_API}?part=statistics&id=${encodeURIComponent(videoId)}&key=${apiKey}`\n\n  const res = await fetch(url)\n  if (!res.ok) {\n    return { statusCode: res.status, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'YouTube API error' }) }\n  }\n\n  const data = await res.json()\n  const item = data.items?.[0]\n\n  if (!item) {\n    return { statusCode: 404, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Video not found' }) }\n  }\n\n  const { viewCount, likeCount, commentCount } = item.statistics\n\n  return {\n    statusCode: 200,\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n    body: JSON.stringify({\n      views:    Number(viewCount    ?? 0),\n      likes:    Number(likeCount    ?? 0),\n      comments: Number(commentCount ?? 0),\n    }),\n  }\n}\n"
}

[tool_use: Write]
{
  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/utils/youtube.ts",
  "content": "/**\n * Extracts the YouTube video ID from common URL formats:\n *   https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VIDEO_ID\n *   https://youtu.be/VIDEO_ID\n *   https://www.youtube.com/shorts/VIDEO_ID\n *   https://www.youtube.com/embed/VIDEO_ID\n *\n * Returns null if the URL doesn't match any known format.\n */\nexport function extractYouTubeId(url: string): string | null {\n  if (!url) return null\n\n  try {\n    const u = new URL(url)\n\n    // youtu.be/ID\n    if (u.hostname === 'youtu.be') {\n      const id = u.pathname.slice(1).split('/')[0]\n      return id || null\n    }\n\n    // youtube.com/watch?v=ID\n    if (u.hostname.endsWith('youtube.com')) {\n      if (u.pathname === '/watch') {\n        return u.searchParams.get('v')\n      }\n      // youtube.com/shorts/ID or youtube.com/embed/ID\n      const match = u.pathname.match(/^\\/(shorts|embed)\\/([^/?]+)/)\n      if (match) return match[2]\n    }\n\n    return null\n  } catch {\n    return null\n  }\n}\n"
}

[tool_use: Write]
{
  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/hooks/useYouTubeStats.ts",
  "content": "import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'\nimport { extractYouTubeId } from '../utils/youtube'\n\nexport interface YouTubeStats {\n  views:    number\n  likes:    number\n  comments: number\n}\n\ninterface Result {\n  stats:   YouTubeStats | null\n  loading: boolean\n  error:   string | null\n  refresh: () => void\n}\n\nexport function useYouTubeStats(liveUrl: string): Result {\n  const [stats,   setStats]   = useState<YouTubeStats | null>(null)\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)\n  const [error,   setError]   = useState<string | null>(null)\n  const [tick,    setTick]    = useState(0)\n\n  const refresh = useCallback(() => setTick((t) => t + 1), [])\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const videoId = extractYouTubeId(liveUrl)\n    if (!videoId) {\n      setStats(null)\n      setError(null)\n      return\n    }\n\n    let cancelled = false\n    setLoading(true)\n    setError(null)\n\n    fetch(`/.netlify/functions/youtube-stats?videoId=${encodeURIComponent(videoId)}`)\n      .then((res) => {\n        if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`)\n        return res.json()\n      })\n      .then((data: YouTubeStats) => {\n        if (!cancelled) { setStats(data); setLoading(false) }\n      })\n      .catch((err: Error) => {\n        if (!cancelled) { setError(err.message); setLoading(false) }\n      })\n\n    return () => { cancelled = true }\n  }, [liveUrl, tick])\n\n  return { stats, loading, error, refresh }\n}\n"
}

--- CLAUDE ---
Clean build. Here's a summary of everything that was implemented:

---

**YouTube API integration — done.** Here's what was built:

**`netlify.toml`** — build config, functions directory, SPA redirect, and dev port.

**`netlify/functions/youtube-stats.ts`** — server-side proxy that reads `YOUTUBE_API_KEY` from `process.env` (never exposed to the client), calls `youtube.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos?part=statistics`, and returns `{ views, likes, comments }`.

**`src/utils/youtube.ts`** — `extractYouTubeId()` handles `youtube.com/watch?v=`, `youtu.be/`, `/shorts/`, and `/embed/` URL formats.

**`src/hooks/useYouTubeStats.ts`** — fetches from `/.netlify/functions/youtube-stats`, returns `{ stats, loading, error, refresh }`. Re-fetches when URL changes or `refresh()` is called.

**`src/types/video.ts`** — added `liveUrl: string` and `perfNote: string` to `Video`; `perfNote` is excluded from `VideoInput`.

**`src/components/pipeline/VideoForm.tsx`** — `liveUrl` input appears only when `stage === 'Published'`.

**`src/components/pipeline/PerformanceCard.tsx`** — shows on Published cards with a live URL set. Displays views/likes/comments with K/M formatting, a `[WATCH]` link, `[REFRESH]` button, and an inline `perfNote` textarea that saves to Firestore on blur.

**`src/components/pipeline/VideoCard.tsx`** — renders `<PerformanceCard>` when `stage === 'Published' && liveUrl`.

To test locally with Netlify Functions running, use `netlify dev` instead of `npm run dev` — that spins up both the Vite dev server and the Functions runtime together, so the `/.netlify/functions/youtube-stats` endpoint is live.

--- YOU ---

--- CLAUDE ---
The problem: `port = 5173` tells Netlify Dev to listen on 5173, but `npm run dev` (Vite) also binds to 5173 — same port, conflict. Netlify Dev needs its own port and a `targetPort` pointing at the Vite process.

--- CLAUDE ---
[tool_use: Edit]
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/netlify.toml",
  "old_string": "[dev]\n  command = \"npm run dev\"\n  port    = 5173",
  "new_string": "[dev]\n  command    = \"npm run dev\"\n  targetPort = 5173\n  port       = 8888"
}

--- YOU ---
[tool_result]
The file /Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/netlify.toml has been updated successfully.

--- CLAUDE ---
- `targetPort = 5173` — where Vite is running
- `port = 8888` — where Netlify Dev listens (proxies Vite + serves functions)

Now run `netlify dev` and open `http://localhost:8888`. The `/.netlify/functions/youtube-stats` endpoint will be available there alongside your app.

import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { AuthProvider } from './context/AuthContext'
import { FilterProvider } from './context/FilterContext'
import ProtectedRoute from './components/ProtectedRoute'
import AppLayout  from './layouts/AppLayout'
import Landing    from './pages/Landing'
import Login      from './pages/Login'
import Dashboard  from './pages/Dashboard'
import Pipeline   from './pages/Pipeline'

export default function App() {
  return (
    <AuthProvider>
      <FilterProvider>
      <BrowserRouter>
        <Routes>
          {/* Public */}
          <Route path="/"      element={<Landing />} />
          <Route path="/login" element={<Login />} />

          {/* Protected — all app pages live under /app */}
          <Route path="/app" element={
            <ProtectedRoute>
              <AppLayout />
            </ProtectedRoute>
          }>
            <Route index element={<Navigate to="dashboard" replace />} />
            <Route path="dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
            <Route path="pipeline"  element={<Pipeline />} />
          </Route>

          {/* Catch-all */}
          <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
        </Routes>
      </BrowserRouter>
      </FilterProvider>
    </AuthProvider>
  )
}

The app code looks fine. The white screen on `netlify dev` is almost always Netlify Dev proxying to Vite before Vite has finished starting up — or Vite's HMR websocket failing through the proxy. Check the browser console first: are there any errors?

Also check: is the white screen at `localhost:8888` specifically, or does `localhost:5173` also show white?

The most common cause is `framework` detection being missing so Netlify Dev doesn't know to wait for Vite to be ready. Add `framework` to the dev config:

--- CLAUDE ---
The `[[redirects]]` catch-all rule is the problem. In dev mode, Netlify's proxy at 8888 intercepts every request — including Vite's module requests for `/src/main.tsx`, `/@vite/client`, etc. — and rewrites them all to `/index.html`. The browser gets HTML where it expected JavaScript, hence the import-analysis error.

In production this rule is safe because actual files in `dist/` shadow it. In dev mode there are no files on disk, so it catches everything.

Fix: scope the SPA redirect to production only, where it belongs. Vite handles SPA fallback itself in dev mode.

--- CLAUDE ---
[tool_use: Read]
{
  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/netlify.toml"
}

     1→[build]
     2→  command   = "npm run build"
     3→  publish   = "dist"
     4→  functions = "netlify/functions"
     5→
     6→[[redirects]]
     7→  from   = "/*"
     8→  to     = "/index.html"
     9→  status = 200
    10→
    11→[dev]
    12→  command    = "npm run dev"
    13→  targetPort = 5173
    14→  port       = 8888
    15→  framework  = "#custom"
    16→

Alright when I put a url into the published video section i see Err: HTTP 403 and a watch link but that's it. Is there a way to connect a specific YouTube channel directly to the site and have a whole section for the statistics

--- CLAUDE ---


--- CLAUDE ---
Two separate things to address:

**The 403 error** — that's coming from YouTube's API, not our code. The API key you created has an HTTP referrer restriction set to your Netlify domain. But when `netlify dev` runs locally, the function makes requests from `localhost`, which doesn't match that restriction. Fix it in Google Cloud Console:

> APIs & Services → Credentials → click your API key → under "Application restrictions", either switch to "None" (fine for a private tool) or add `localhost/*` to the allowed referrers.

Then restart `netlify dev`.

---

**Connecting a channel for a full stats section** — yes, absolutely. The YouTube Data API v3 has a `channels.list` endpoint that returns subscriber count, total view count, and video count for any channel ID. No OAuth needed — same API key, same proxy pattern.

This would look like a new **Channel Stats** page with:
- Subscriber count, total views, total videos (from the channel)
- A table of recent published videos with their per-video stats pulled from Firestore (already have `liveUrl` on each card, so we have the video IDs)

Want me to build that out? If so, a couple of quick questions:
1. Do you have both Pab and Opher's channel IDs? (Found in YouTube Studio → Settings → Channel → Advanced, or from the channel URL)
2. Is this one shared channel or two separate channels?

That determines whether the stats page shows one set of numbers or a side-by-side comparison.

     1→import type { Handler, HandlerEvent } from '@netlify/functions'
     2→
     3→const YT_API = 'https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos'
     4→
     5→export const handler: Handler = async (event: HandlerEvent) => {
     6→  const videoId = event.queryStringParameters?.videoId
     7→
     8→  if (!videoId) {
     9→    return { statusCode: 400, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Missing videoId' }) }
    10→  }
    11→
    12→  const apiKey = process.env.YOUTUBE_API_KEY
    13→  if (!apiKey) {
    14→    return { statusCode: 500, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'API key not configured' }) }
    15→  }
    16→
    17→  const url = `${YT_API}?part=statistics&id=${encodeURIComponent(videoId)}&key=${apiKey}`
    18→
    19→  const res = await fetch(url)
    20→  if (!res.ok) {
    21→    return { statusCode: res.status, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'YouTube API error' }) }
    22→  }
    23→
    24→  const data = await res.json()
    25→  const item = data.items?.[0]
    26→
    27→  if (!item) {
    28→    return { statusCode: 404, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Video not found' }) }
    29→  }
    30→
    31→  const { viewCount, likeCount, commentCount } = item.statistics
    32→
    33→  return {
    34→    statusCode: 200,
    35→    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    36→    body: JSON.stringify({
    37→      views:    Number(viewCount    ?? 0),
    38→      likes:    Number(likeCount    ?? 0),
    39→      comments: Number(commentCount ?? 0),
    40→    }),
    41→  }
    42→}
    43→

--- CLAUDE ---
Restart `netlify dev` and trigger the error again. The logs will appear in the terminal where `netlify dev` is running — look for lines starting with `[youtube-stats]`. Paste what you see and I'll tell you exactly what's wrong.

The most likely culprits given an unrestricted key:
- **`YOUTUBE_API_KEY` not being read** — `netlify dev` reads `.env`, not `.env.local`. If the key is only in `.env.local`, the function gets `undefined` and the request goes out with a literal `undefined` in the URL. Check the log line `apiKey present: false`.
- **YouTube Data API v3 not enabled** for this project in Google Cloud Console (403 with `accessNotConfigured` in the error body).

The `detail` field in the error response will now show the full YouTube error message, which will make it obvious.

--- CLAUDE ---
The key is still set to "HTTP referrers" restriction type in Google Cloud Console — you cleared the list but didn't switch the restriction type to **None**. Server-side functions never send a `Referer` header, so Google sees `<empty>` and blocks it.

**Fix in Google Cloud Console:**
APIs & Services → Credentials → click the key → under "Application restrictions" → select the **None** radio button (not just clear the referrer list) → Save.

Takes 1–5 minutes to propagate.

**Immediate workaround** — add a `Referer` header to the outgoing fetch so it matches whatever restriction you had set:

--- CLAUDE ---

--- CLAUDE ---
Now add `SITE_URL` to your `.env` file (not `.env.local`):

```
SITE_URL=https://your-site.netlify.app
```

Netlify automatically sets `SITE_URL` in production, so you only need it locally. Set the value to whatever domain you had in the HTTP referrer restriction, restart `netlify dev`, and it'll work immediately while you wait for the "None" setting to propagate.

Once the restriction is set to None and propagated, the `Referer` header becomes a no-op and nothing needs to change.

  "content": "import type { Handler, HandlerEvent } from '@netlify/functions'\n\nconst YT_CHANNELS = 'https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/channels'\nconst YT_VIDEOS   = 'https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos'\n\nexport const handler: Handler = async (event: HandlerEvent) => {\n  const apiKey    = process.env.YOUTUBE_API_KEY\n  const channelId = process.env.YOUTUBE_CHANNEL_ID\n  const videoIds  = event.queryStringParameters?.videoIds  // optional, comma-separated\n  const referer   = process.env.SITE_URL ?? 'https://localhost'\n\n  if (!apiKey)    return { statusCode: 500, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'API key not configured' }) }\n  if (!channelId) return { statusCode: 500, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Channel ID not configured' }) }\n\n  const headers = { Referer: referer }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500 Channel stats \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const channelUrl = `${YT_CHANNELS}?part=statistics&id=${channelId}&key=${apiKey}`\n  const channelRes = await fetch(channelUrl, { headers })\n\n  if (!channelRes.ok) {\n    const detail = await channelRes.text()\n    return { statusCode: channelRes.status, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Channel API error', detail }) }\n  }\n\n  const channelData = await channelRes.json()\n  const s = channelData.items?.[0]?.statistics ?? {}\n\n  const channel = {\n    subscribers: Number(s.subscriberCount ?? 0),\n    views:       Number(s.viewCount       ?? 0),\n    videoCount:  Number(s.videoCount      ?? 0),\n  }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500 Batch video stats (optional) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const videos: Record<string, { views: number; likes: number; comments: number }> = {}\n\n  if (videoIds) {\n    const videosUrl = `${YT_VIDEOS}?part=statistics&id=${encodeURIComponent(videoIds)}&key=${apiKey}`\n    const videosRes = await fetch(videosUrl, { headers })\n\n    if (videosRes.ok) {\n      const videosData = await videosRes.json()\n      for (const item of videosData.items ?? []) {\n        videos[item.id] = {\n          views:    Number(item.statistics.viewCount    ?? 0),\n          likes:    Number(item.statistics.likeCount    ?? 0),\n          comments: Number(item.statistics.commentCount ?? 0),\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  return {\n    statusCode: 200,\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n    body: JSON.stringify({ channel, videos }),\n  }\n}\n"
}

{
  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/hooks/useChannelAnalytics.ts",
  "content": "import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'\n\nexport interface ChannelStats {\n  subscribers: number\n  views:       number\n  videoCount:  number\n}\n\nexport interface VideoStat {\n  views:    number\n  likes:    number\n  comments: number\n}\n\nexport interface ChannelAnalytics {\n  channel: ChannelStats\n  videos:  Record<string, VideoStat>  // keyed by YouTube video ID\n}\n\ninterface Result {\n  data:    ChannelAnalytics | null\n  loading: boolean\n  error:   string | null\n  refresh: () => void\n}\n\n/**\n * Fetches channel-level stats plus per-video stats in one call.\n * @param videoIdsParam  Comma-separated YouTube video IDs (empty string = channel only)\n */\nexport function useChannelAnalytics(videoIdsParam: string): Result {\n  const [data,    setData]    = useState<ChannelAnalytics | null>(null)\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n  const [error,   setError]   = useState<string | null>(null)\n  const [tick,    setTick]    = useState(0)\n\n  const refresh = useCallback(() => setTick((t) => t + 1), [])\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let cancelled = false\n    setLoading(true)\n    setError(null)\n\n    const params = videoIdsParam ? `?videoIds=${encodeURIComponent(videoIdsParam)}` : ''\n\n    fetch(`/.netlify/functions/youtube-analytics${params}`)\n      .then((res) => {\n        if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`)\n        return res.json()\n      })\n      .then((d: ChannelAnalytics) => {\n        if (!cancelled) { setData(d); setLoading(false) }\n      })\n      .catch((err: Error) => {\n        if (!cancelled) { setError(err.message); setLoading(false) }\n      })\n\n    return () => { cancelled = true }\n  }, [videoIdsParam, tick])\n\n  return { data, loading, error, refresh }\n}\n"
}

  "content": "import { useEffect, useMemo } from 'react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport type { Video } from '../types/video'\nimport { subscribeToVideos } from '../firebase/videos'\nimport { useFilter } from '../context/FilterContext'\nimport { extractYouTubeId } from '../utils/youtube'\nimport { useChannelAnalytics } from '../hooks/useChannelAnalytics'\n\nfunction fmt(n: number): string {\n  if (n >= 1_000_000) return `${(n / 1_000_000).toFixed(1)}M`\n  if (n >= 1_000)     return `${(n / 1_000).toFixed(1)}K`\n  return n.toLocaleString()\n}\n\nexport default function Stats() {\n  const [videos, setVideos] = useState<Video[]>([])\n  const { activeCreator }   = useFilter()\n\n  useEffect(() => subscribeToVideos(setVideos), [])\n\n  // Published videos with a live URL\n  const publishedVideos = useMemo(() => {\n    let result = videos.filter((v) => v.stage === 'Published' && v.liveUrl)\n    if (activeCreator !== 'All') result = result.filter((v) => v.creator === activeCreator)\n    return result\n  }, [videos, activeCreator])\n\n  // Map: firestoreId \u2192 youtubeId\n  const idMap = useMemo(() => {\n    const map: Record<string, string> = {}\n    for (const v of publishedVideos) {\n      const ytId = extractYouTubeId(v.liveUrl)\n      if (ytId) map[v.id] = ytId\n    }\n    return map\n  }, [publishedVideos])\n\n  // Reverse map: youtubeId \u2192 firestoreId (for looking up stats by video)\n  const reverseMap = useMemo(() => {\n    const map: Record<string, string> = {}\n    for (const [fsId, ytId] of Object.entries(idMap)) map[ytId] = fsId\n    return map\n  }, [idMap])\n\n  const videoIdsParam = Object.values(idMap).join(',')\n\n  const { data, loading, error, refresh } = useChannelAnalytics(videoIdsParam)\n\n  const channel = data?.channel\n  const ytStats = data?.videos ?? {}\n\n  // Build display rows: pair Firestore video data with YouTube stats\n  const rows = useMemo(() => {\n    return publishedVideos\n      .map((v) => {\n        const ytId  = idMap[v.id]\n        const stats = ytId ? ytStats[ytId] : undefined\n        return { video: v, ytId, stats }\n      })\n      .sort((a, b) => (b.stats?.views ?? 0) - (a.stats?.views ?? 0))\n  }, [publishedVideos, idMap, ytStats])\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"stats-page\">\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Channel overview \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */}\n      <div className=\"stats-section\">\n        <div className=\"stats-section-header\">\n          <h2 className=\"stats-heading\">CHANNEL STATS</h2>\n          <button className=\"stats-refresh-btn\" onClick={refresh} disabled={loading}>\n            {loading ? 'LOADING...' : '[REFRESH]'}\n          </button>\n        </div>\n\n        {error && <p className=\"stats-error\">ERR: {error}</p>}\n\n        <div className=\"channel-overview\">\n          <div className=\"channel-stat-block\">\n            <span className=\"channel-stat-value\">\n              {channel ? fmt(channel.subscribers) : '\u2014'}\n            </span>\n            <span className=\"channel-stat-label\">SUBSCRIBERS</span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"channel-stat-divider\">|</div>\n          <div className=\"channel-stat-block\">\n            <span className=\"channel-stat-value\">\n              {channel ? fmt(channel.views) : '\u2014'}\n            </span>\n            <span className=\"channel-stat-label\">TOTAL VIEWS</span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"channel-stat-divider\">|</div>\n          <div className=\"channel-stat-block\">\n            <span className=\"channel-stat-value\">\n              {channel ? fmt(channel.videoCount) : '\u2014'}\n            </span>\n            <span className=\"channel-stat-label\">VIDEOS</span>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Per-video performance \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */}\n      <div className=\"stats-section\">\n        <div className=\"stats-section-header\">\n          <h2 className=\"stats-heading\">VIDEO PERFORMANCE</h2>\n          {activeCreator !== 'All' && (\n            <span className={`stats-filter-badge creator-tag-${activeCreator.toLowerCase()}`}>\n              {activeCreator.toUpperCase()} ONLY\n            </span>\n          )}\n        </div>\n\n        {rows.length === 0 && !loading && (\n          <p className=\"stats-empty\">\n            {activeCreator === 'All'\n              ? 'No published videos with a live URL yet. Add a YouTube URL to a Published card.'\n              : `No published videos with a live URL for ${activeCreator}.`}\n          </p>\n        )}\n\n        {rows.length > 0 && (\n          <div className=\"stats-table-wrap\">\n            <table className=\"stats-table\">\n              <thead>\n                <tr>\n                  <th>TITLE</th>\n                  <th>CREATOR</th>\n                  <th className=\"stat-col\">VIEWS</th>\n                  <th className=\"stat-col\">LIKES</th>\n                  <th className=\"stat-col\">CMTS</th>\n                  <th className=\"stat-col\">LINK</th>\n                </tr>\n              </thead>\n              <tbody>\n                {rows.map(({ video, ytId, stats }) => (\n                  <tr key={video.id}>\n                    <td className=\"stats-title-cell\">{video.title}</td>\n                    <td>\n                      <span className={`creator-tag creator-tag-${video.creator.toLowerCase()}`}>\n                        {video.creator.toUpperCase()}\n                      </span>\n                    </td>\n                    <td className=\"stat-col stat-value\">\n                      {stats ? fmt(stats.views) : (loading ? - **Top section** — Subscribers, Total Views, Videos pulled live from the channel

[tool_result]
     1→import type { Handler, HandlerEvent } from '@netlify/functions'
     2→
     3→const YT_CHANNELS = 'https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/channels'
     4→const YT_VIDEOS   = 'https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/videos'
     5→
     6→export const handler: Handler = async (event: HandlerEvent) => {
     7→  const apiKey    = process.env.YOUTUBE_API_KEY
     8→  const channelId = process.env.YOUTUBE_CHANNEL_ID
     9→  const videoIds  = event.queryStringParameters?.videoIds  // optional, comma-separated
    10→  const referer   = process.env.SITE_URL ?? 'https://localhost'
    11→
    12→  console.log('[youtube-analytics] apiKey present:', !!apiKey, '| channelId:', channelId ?? 'MISSING')
    13→
    14→  if (!apiKey)    return { statusCode: 500, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'API key not configured' }) }
    15→  if (!channelId) return { statusCode: 500, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Channel ID not configured — set YOUTUBE_CHANNEL_ID in .env' }) }
    16→
    17→  const headers = { Referer: referer }
    18→
    19→  // ── Channel stats ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    20→  const channelUrl = `${YT_CHANNELS}?part=statistics&id=${channelId}&key=${apiKey}`
    21→  const channelRes = await fetch(channelUrl, { headers })
    22→
    23→  if (!channelRes.ok) {
    24→    const detail = await channelRes.text()
    25→    return { statusCode: channelRes.status, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Channel API error', detail }) }
    26→  }
    27→
    28→  const channelData = await channelRes.json()
    29→  const s = channelData.items?.[0]?.statistics ?? {}
    30→
    31→  const channel = {
    32→    subscribers: Number(s.subscriberCount ?? 0),
    33→    views:       Number(s.viewCount       ?? 0),
    34→    videoCount:  Number(s.videoCount      ?? 0),
    35→  }
    36→
    37→  // ── Batch video stats (optional) ──────────────────────────────────────────
    38→  const videos: Record<string, { views: number; likes: number; comments: number }> = {}
    39→
    40→  if (videoIds) {
    41→    const videosUrl = `${YT_VIDEOS}?part=statistics&id=${encodeURIComponent(videoIds)}&key=${apiKey}`
    42→    const videosRes = await fetch(videosUrl, { headers })
    43→
    44→    if (videosRes.ok) {
    45→      const videosData = await videosRes.json()
    46→      for (const item of videosData.items ?? []) {
    47→        videos[item.id] = {
    48→          views:    Number(item.statistics.viewCount    ?? 0),
    49→          likes:    Number(item.statistics.likeCount    ?? 0),
    50→          comments: Number(item.statistics.commentCount ?? 0),
    51→        }
    52→      }
    53→    }
    54→  }
    55→
    56→  return {
    57→    statusCode: 200,
    58→    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    59→    body: JSON.stringify({ channel, videos }),
    60→  }
    61→}
    62→

[tool_result]
     1→import { useEffect, useMemo } from 'react'
     2→import { useState } from 'react'
     3→import type { Video } from '../types/video'
     4→import { subscribeToVideos } from '../firebase/videos'
     5→import { useFilter } from '../context/FilterContext'
     6→import { extractYouTubeId } from '../utils/youtube'
     7→import { useChannelAnalytics } from '../hooks/useChannelAnalytics'
     8→
     9→function fmt(n: number): string {
    10→  if (n >= 1_000_000) return `${(n / 1_000_000).toFixed(1)}M`
    11→  if (n >= 1_000)     return `${(n / 1_000).toFixed(1)}K`
    12→  return n.toLocaleString()
    13→}
    14→
    15→export default function Stats() {
    16→  const [videos, setVideos] = useState<Video[]>([])
    17→  const { activeCreator }   = useFilter()
    18→
    19→  useEffect(() => subscribeToVideos(setVideos), [])
    20→
    21→  // Published videos with a live URL
    22→  const publishedVideos = useMemo(() => {
    23→    let result = videos.filter((v) => v.stage === 'Published' && v.liveUrl)
    24→    if (activeCreator !== 'All') result = result.filter((v) => v.creator === activeCreator)
    25→    return result
    26→  }, [videos, activeCreator])
    27→
    28→  // Map: firestoreId → youtubeId
    29→  const idMap = useMemo(() => {
    30→    const map: Record<string, string> = {}
    31→    for (const v of publishedVideos) {
    32→      const ytId = extractYouTubeId(v.liveUrl)
    33→      if (ytId) map[v.id] = ytId
    34→    }
    35→    return map
    36→  }, [publishedVideos])
    37→
    38→  const videoIdsParam = Object.values(idMap).join(',')
    39→
    40→  const { data, loading, error, refresh } = useChannelAnalytics(videoIdsParam)
    41→
    42→  const channel = data?.channel
    43→  const ytStats = data?.videos ?? {}
    44→
    45→  // Build display rows: pair Firestore video data with YouTube stats
    46→  const rows = useMemo(() => {
    47→    return publishedVideos
    48→      .map((v) => {
    49→        const ytId  = idMap[v.id]
    50→        const stats = ytId ? ytStats[ytId] : undefined
    51→        return { video: v, ytId, stats }
    52→      })
    53→      .sort((a, b) => (b.stats?.views ?? 0) - (a.stats?.views ?? 0))
    54→  }, [publishedVideos, idMap, ytStats])
    55→
    56→  return (
    57→    <div className="stats-page">
    58→
    59→      {/* ── Channel overview ─────────────────────────────── */}

'https://localhost'\n\n  console.log('[youtube-analytics] apiKey present:', !!apiKey, '| channelId:', channelId ?? 'MISSING')\n\n  if (!apiKey)    return { statusCode: 500, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'API key not configured' }) }\n  if (!channelId) return { statusCode: 500, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Channel ID not configured \u2014 set YOUTUBE_CHANNEL_ID in .env' }) }\n\n  const headers = { Referer: referer }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500 1. Channel stats + uploads playlist ID \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const channelUrl = `${YT_CHANNELS}?part=statistics,contentDetails&id=${channelId}&key=${apiKey}`\n  const channelRes = await fetch(channelUrl, { headers })\n\n  if (!channelRes.ok) {\n    const detail = await channelRes.text()\n    return { statusCode: channelRes.status, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Channel API error', detail }) }\n  }\n\n  const channelData  = await channelRes.json()\n  const channelItem  = channelData.items?.[0]\n  const s            = channelItem?.statistics ?? {}\n  const uploadsId: string | undefined = channelItem?.contentDetails?.relatedPlaylists?.uploads\n\n  const channel = {\n    subscribers: Number(s.subscriberCount ?? 0),\n    views:       Number(s.viewCount       ?? 0),\n    videoCount:  Number(s.videoCount      ?? 0),\n  }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500 2. Fetch uploads playlist (50 most recent) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  let uploadedVideos: {\n    id: string; title: string; thumbnail: string\n    publishedAt: string; views: number; likes: number; comments: number\n  }[] = []\n\n  if (uploadsId) {\n    const playlistUrl = `${YT_PLAYLIST_ITEMS}?part=snippet&playlistId=${uploadsId}&maxResults=50&key=${apiKey}`\n    const playlistRes = await fetch(playlistUrl, { headers })\n\n    if (playlistRes.ok) {\n      const playlistData = await playlistRes.json()\n      const items = (playlistData.items ?? []) as {\n        snippet: {\n          resourceId: { videoId: string }\n          title: string\n          publishedAt: string\n          thumbnails: Record<string, { url: string }>\n        }\n      }[]\n\n      // Filter out deleted/private placeholders\n      const validItems = items.filter((i) => i.snippet.title !== 'Deleted video' && i.snippet.title !== 'Private video')\n      const uploadIds  = validItems.map((i) => i.snippet.resourceId.videoId).join(',')\n\n      // \u2500\u2500 3. Batch-fetch stats for those videos \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n      if (uploadIds) {\n        const statsUrl = `${YT_VIDEOS}?part=statistics&id=${encodeURIComponent(uploadIds)}&key=${apiKey}`\n        const statsRes = await fetch(statsUrl, { headers })\n\n        const statsMap: Record<string, { viewCount: string; likeCount: string; commentCount: string }> = {}\n        if (statsRes.ok) {\n          const statsData = await statsRes.json()\n          for (const item of statsData.items ?? []) {\n            statsMap[item.id] = item.statistics\n          }\n        }\n\n        uploadedVideos = validItems.map((item) => {\n          const id     = item.snippet.resourceId.videoId\n          const stats  = statsMap[id] ?? {}\n          const thumbs = item.snippet.thumbnails\n          return {\n            id,\n            title:       item.snippet.title,\n            thumbnail:   thumbs.medium?.url ?? thumbs.default?.url ?? '',\n            publishedAt: item.snippet.publishedAt,\n            views:       Number(stats.viewCount    ?? 0),\n            likes:       Number(stats.likeCount    ?? 0),\n            comments:    Number(stats.commentCount ?? 0),\n          }\n        })\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // \u2500\u2500 4. Pipeline video stats (optional, for the performance table) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  const videos: Record<string, { views: number; likes: number; comments: number }> = {}\n\n  if (videoIds) {\n    const videosUrl = `${YT_VIDEOS}?part=statistics&id=${encodeURIComponent(videoIds)}&key=${apiKey}`\n    const videosRes = await fetch(videosUrl, { headers })\n\n    if (videosRes.ok) {\n      const videosData = await videosRes.json()\n      for (const item of videosData.items ?? []) {\n        videos[item.id] = {\n          views:    Number(item.statistics.viewCount    ?? 0),\n          likes:    Number(item.statistics.likeCount    ?? 0),\n          comments: Number(item.statistics.commentCount ?? 0),\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  return {\n    statusCode: 200,\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n    body: JSON.stringify({ channel, uploadedVideos, videos }),\n  }\n}\n"

{
  "file_path": "/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/src/hooks/useChannelAnalytics.ts",
  "content": "import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'\n\nexport interface ChannelStats {\n  subscribers: number\n  views:       number\n  videoCount:  number\n}\n\nexport interface VideoStat {\n  views:    number\n  likes:    number\n  comments: number\n}\n\nexport interface UploadedVideo {\n  id:          string\n  title:       string\n  thumbnail:   string\n  publishedAt: string   // ISO 8601\n  views:       number\n  likes:       number\n  comments:    number\n}\n\nexport interface ChannelAnalytics {\n  channel:        ChannelStats\n  uploadedVideos: UploadedVideo[]\n  videos:         Record<string, VideoStat>  // keyed by YouTube video ID\n}\n\ninterface Result {\n  data:    ChannelAnalytics | null\n  loading: boolean\n  error:   string | null\n  refresh: () => void\n}\n\nexport function useChannelAnalytics(videoIdsParam: string): Result {\n  const [data,    setData]    = useState<ChannelAnalytics | null>(null)\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n  const [error,   setError]   = useState<string | null>(null)\n  const [tick,    setTick]    = useState(0)\n\n  const refresh = useCallback(() => setTick((t) => t + 1), [])\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let cancelled = false\n    setLoading(true)\n    setError(null)\n\n    const params = videoIdsParam ? `?videoIds=${encodeURIComponent(videoIdsParam)}` : ''\n\n    fetch(`/.netlify/functions/youtube-analytics${params}`)\n      .then((res) => {\n        if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`)\n        return res.json()\n      })\n      .then((d: ChannelAnalytics) => {\n        if (!cancelled) { setData(d); setLoading(false) }\n      })\n      .catch((err: Error) => {\n        if (!cancelled) { setError(err.message); setLoading(false) }\n      })\n\n    return () => { cancelled = true }\n  }, [videoIdsParam, tick])\n\n  return { data, loading, error, refresh }\n}\n"
}

(const v of publishedVideos) {\n      const ytId = extractYouTubeId(v.liveUrl)\n      if (ytId) map[v.id] = ytId\n    }\n    return map\n  }, [publishedVideos])\n\n  const videoIdsParam = performance table rows\n  const rows = useMemo(() => {\n    return publishedVideos\n      .map((v) => {\n        const ytId  = idMap[v.id]\n        const stats = ytId ? ytStats[ytId] : undefined\n key\n  const sortedUploads = useMemo(() => {\n    const list = [...(data?.uploadedVideos ?? Update `src/hooks/useChannelAnalytics.ts`\n\nAdd `isShort: boolean` to `UploadedVideo`. Replace the entire file with:\n\n```typescript\nimport { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'\n\nexport interface ChannelStats {\n  subscribers: number\n  views:       number\n  videoCount:  number\n}\n\nexport interface VideoStat {\n  views:    number\n  likes:    number\n  comments: number\n}\n\nexport interface UploadedVideo {\n  id:          string\n  title:       string\n  thumbnail:   string\n  publishedAt: string\n  isShort:     boolean\n  views:       number\n  likes:       number\n  comments:    number\n}\n\nexport interface ChannelAnalytics {\n  channel:        ChannelStats\n  uploadedVideos: UploadedVideo[]\n  videos:         Record<string, VideoStat>\n}\n\ninterface Result {\n  data:    ChannelAnalytics | null\n  loading: boolean\n  error:   string | null\n  refresh: () => void\n}\n\nexport function useChannelAnalytics(videoIdsParam: string): Result {\n  const [data,    setData]    = useState<ChannelAnalytics | null>(null)\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n  const [error,   setError]   = useState<string | null>(null)\n  const [tick,    setTick]    = useState(0)\n\n  const refresh = useCallback(() => setTick((t) => t + 1), [])\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let cancelled = false\n    setLoading(true)\n    setError(null)\n\n    const params = videoIdsParam ? `?videoIds=${encodeURIComponent(videoIdsParam)}` : ''\n\n    fetch(`/.netlify/functions/youtube-analytics${params}`)\n      .then((res) => {\n        if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`)\n        return res.json()\n      })\n      .then((d: ChannelAnalytics) => {\n        if (!cancelled) { setData(d); setLoading(false) }\n      })\n      .catch((err: Error) => {\n        if (!cancelled) { setError(err.message); setLoading(false) }\n      })\n\n    return () => { cancelled = true }\n  }, [videoIdsParam, tick])\n\n  return { data, loading, error, refresh }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Create `src/firebase/channelVideos.ts`\n\nNew file. Stores creator assignments (Pab/Opher) for YouTube uploaded videos, keyed by YouTube video ID.\n\n```typescript\nimport {\n  collection,\n  doc,\n  setDoc,\n  deleteDoc,\n  onSnapshot,\n} from 'firebase/firestore'\nimport { db } from './config'\nimport type { Creator } from '../types/video'\n\nconst COL = collection(db, 'channelVideos')\n\n/**\n * Subscribes to all creator assignments.\n * Returns a map of { youtubeVideoId: Creator }.\n */\nexport function subscribeToChannelVideos(\n  onChange: (assignments: Record<string, Creator>) => void\n): () => void {\n  return onSnapshot(COL, (snap) => {\n    const map: Record<string, Creator> = {}\n    for (const d of snap.docs) {\n      map[d.id] = d.data().creator as Creator\n    }\n    onChange(map)\n  })\n}\n\n/** Assigns a creator to a YouTube video. */\nexport function setVideoCreator(videoId: string, creator: Creator): Promise<void> {\n  return setDoc(doc(COL, videoId), { creator })\n}\n\n/** Removes the creator assignment from a YouTube video. */\nexport function clearVideoCreator(videoId: string): Promise<void> {\n  return deleteDoc(doc(COL, videoId))\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. One thing to paste into the Firebase Console → Firestore → Rules tab — the `channelVideos` rule was added to `firestore.rules` locally but the live rules still need to be updated:

```
rules_version = '2';
service cloud.firestore {
  match /databases/{database}/documents {
    match /videos/{videoId} {
      allow read, write: if request.auth != null;
    }
    match /workspace/{docId} {
      allow read, write: if request.auth != null;
    }
    match /channelVideos/{videoId} {
      allow read, write: if request.auth != null;
    }
  }
}
```

[tool_result]
     1→import {
     2→  collection,
     3→  doc,
     4→  setDoc,
     5→  deleteDoc,
     6→  onSnapshot,
     7→} from 'firebase/firestore'
     8→import { db } from './config'
     9→import type { Creator } from '../types/video'
    10→
    11→const COL = collection(db, 'channelVideos')
    12→
    13→/**
    14→ * Subscribes to all creator assignments.
    15→ * Returns a map of { youtubeVideoId: Creator }.
    16→ */
    17→export function subscribeToChannelVideos(
    18→  onChange: (assignments: Record<string, Creator>) => void
    19→): () => void {
    20→  return onSnapshot(COL, (snap) => {
    21→    const map: Record<string, Creator> = {}
    22→    for (const d of snap.docs) {
    23→      map[d.id] = d.data().creator as Creator
    24→    }
    25→    onChange(map)
    26→  })
    27→}
    28→
    29→/** Assigns a creator to a YouTube video. */
    30→export function setVideoCreator(videoId: string, creator: Creator): Promise<void> {
    31→  return setDoc(doc(COL, videoId), { creator })
    32→}
    33→
    34→/** Removes the creator assignment from a YouTube video. */
    35→export function clearVideoCreator(videoId: string): Promise<void> {
    36→  return deleteDoc(doc(COL, videoId))
    37→}
    38→

'...' : 'PAB'}\n              </button>\n              <button\n                className=\"upload-assign-btn upload-assign-opher\"\n                onClick={() => handleAssign('Opher')}\n                disabled={saving}\n              >\n                {saving ? '...' : 'OPHER'}\n              </button>\n            </>\n          )}\n        </div>\n        {err && <p className=\"upload-assign-err\">{err}</p>}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}"
}

--- CLAUDE ---
Clean. Now click a button — if the Firestore rule is missing you'll see a red error message on the card instead of silence. It'll say something like `Missing or insufficient permissions`.

**The fix is almost certainly the Firestore rules.** Go to Firebase Console → Firestore Database → Rules tab and add the `channelVideos` collection:

```
match /channelVideos/{videoId} {
  allow read, write: if request.auth != null;
}
```

Publish the rules, then click PAB or OPHER on any card and it should save immediately with the colored badge appearing.

   104→export default function Stats() {
   105→  const [videos,      setVideos]      = useState<Video[]>([])
   106→  const [assignments, setAssignments] = useState<Record<string, Creator>>({})
   107→  const [typeFilter,  setTypeFilter]  = useState<TypeFilter>('all')
   108→  const [uploadSort,  setUploadSort]  = useState<UploadSort>('date')
   109→  const { activeCreator } = useFilter()
   110→
   111→  useEffect(() => subscribeToVideos(setVideos), [])
   112→  useEffect(() => subscribeToChannelVideos(setAssignments), [])
   113→
   114→  // Pipeline: published videos with a live URL
   115→  const publishedVideos = useMemo(() => {
   116→    let result = videos.filter((v) => v.stage === 'Published' && v.liveUrl)
   117→    if (activeCreator !== 'All') result = result.filter((v) => v.creator === activeCreator)
   118→    return result
   119→  }, [videos, activeCreator])
   120→
   121→  const idMap = useMemo(() => {
   122→    const map: Record<string, string> = {}
   123→    for (const v of publishedVideos) {
   124→      const ytId = extractYouTubeId(v.liveUrl)
   125→      if (ytId) map[v.id] = ytId
   126→    }
   127→    return map
   128→  }, [publishedVideos])
   129→
   130→  const videoIdsParam = Object.values(idMap).join(',')
   131→  const { data, loading, error, refresh } = useChannelAnalytics(videoIdsParam)
   132→
   133→  const channel = data?.channel
   134→  const ytStats = data?.videos ?? {}
   135→
   136→  // Pipeline performance table rows
   137→  const rows = useMemo(() => {
   138→    return publishedVideos
   139→      .map((v) => {
   140→        const ytId  = idMap[v.id]
   141→        const stats = ytId ? ytStats[ytId] : undefined
   142→        return { video: v, ytId, stats }
   143→      })
   144→      .sort((a, b) => (b.stats?.views ?? 0) - (a.stats?.views ?? 0))
   145→  }, [publishedVideos, idMap, ytStats])
   146→
   147→  // Uploaded videos: apply type + creator filters, then sort
   148→  const sortedUploads = useMemo(() => {
   149→    let list = [...(data?.uploadedVideos ?? [])]
   150→
   151→    // Type filter
   152→    if (typeFilter === 'videos') list = list.filter((v) => !v.isShort)
   153→    if (typeFilter === 'shorts') list = list.filter((v) => v.isShort)
   154→
   155→    // Global creator filter — only show videos assigned to that creator (unassigned = hidden)

--- CLAUDE ---
Clean. Here's how it now works:

- **ALL selected** → `CHANNEL STATS`: Subscribers | Total Views | Videos (same as before)
- **PAB selected** → `PAB STATS`: Total Views | Total Likes | Videos | Shorts — all aggregated from only the videos you've tagged as Pab
- **OPHER selected** → `OPHER STATS`: same breakdown for Opher's assigned videos

The individual stats update in real time as you assign more videos — no refresh needed, since it's computed directly from the `assignments` Firestore subscription already running on the page.

     1→import type { Creator } from '../types/video'
     2→
     3→/**
     4→ * Maps a Firebase Auth email to a creator name using env vars.
     5→ * Add VITE_PAB_EMAIL and VITE_OPHER_EMAIL to your .env.local.
     6→ * Returns null if the email doesn't match either — voting is disabled in that case.
     7→ */
     8→export function creatorFromEmail(email: string | null | undefined): Creator | null {
     9→  if (!email) return null
    10→  if (email === import.meta.env.VITE_PAB_EMAIL)   return 'Pab'
    11→  if (email === import.meta.env.VITE_OPHER_EMAIL) return 'Opher'

    13→}

[tool_result]
     1→import { doc, onSnapshot, runTransaction } from 'firebase/firestore'
     2→import { db } from './config'
     3→import type { Creator } from '../types/video'
     4→import type { Workspace } from '../types/workspace'
     5→import { WORKSPACE_DEFAULTS } from '../types/workspace'
     6→
     7→const WORKSPACE_REF = doc(db, 'workspace', 'main')
     8→
     9→// ── Date helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    10→
    11→/** Local date as 'YYYY-MM-DD' — avoids UTC offset shifting the date. */
    12→function localDateString(date: Date): string {
    13→  const y = date.getFullYear()
    14→  const m = String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')
    15→  const d = String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')
    16→  return `${y}-${m}-${d}`
    17→}
    18→
    19→/**
    20→ * Returns the Monday of the ISO week containing the given date (local time).
    21→ * Sunday is treated as the last day of the previous week.
    22→ */
    23→function getWeekStart(date: Date): string {
    24→  const d   = new Date(date)
    25→  const day = d.getDay()                  // 0=Sun, 1=Mon … 6=Sat
    26→  const diff = day === 0 ? -6 : 1 - day  // shift back to Monday
    27→  d.setDate(d.getDate() + diff)
    28→  return localDateString(d)
    29→}
    30→
    31→/** Returns the Monday of the week before the given week-start date. */
    32→function prevWeekStart(weekStart: string): string {
    33→  const d = new Date(weekStart + 'T12:00:00') // noon avoids DST edge cases
    34→  d.setDate(d.getDate() - 7)
    35→  return localDateString(d)
    36→}
    37→
    38→// ── Subscription ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    39→
    40→export function subscribeToWorkspace(onChange: (ws: Workspace) => void): () => void {
    41→  return onSnapshot(WORKSPACE_REF, (snap) => {
    42→    onChange(snap.exists() ? (snap.data() as Workspace) : { ...WORKSPACE_DEFAULTS })
    43→  })
    44→}
    45→
    46→// ── Streak logic ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    47→
    48→/**
    49→ * Records a publish for one creator.
    50→ * - Each creator has their own independent streak.
    51→ * - Streak tracks consecutive calendar weeks (Mon–Sun), any day of the week.
    52→ * - Calling this multiple times in the same week is idempotent.
    53→ * - Confetti is always triggered by the caller regardless of streak changes.
    54→ */
    55→export async function recordPublish(creator: Creator): Promise<void> {
    56→  const weekStart = getWeekStart(new Date())
    57→
    58→  await runTransaction(db, async (tx) => {
    59→    const snap    = await tx.get(WORKSPACE_REF)
    60→    const current: Workspace = snap.exists()
    61→      ? (snap.data() as Workspace)
    62→      : { ...WORKSPACE_DEFAULTS }
    63→
    64→    const existing = current.streaks?.[creator] ?? { count: 0, lastWeekStart: null }
    65→
    66→    // Already published this week — no change needed
    67→    if (existing.lastWeekStart === weekStart) return
    68→
    69→    const wasConsecutive = existing.lastWeekStart === prevWeekStart(weekStart)
    70→
    71→    tx.set(WORKSPACE_REF, {
    72→      ...current,
    73→      streaks: {
    74→        ...current.streaks,
    75→        [creator]: {
    76→          count:         wasConsecutive ? existing.count + 1 : 1,
    77→          lastWeekStart: weekStart,
    78→        },
    79→      },
    80→    })
    81→  })
    82→}
    83→

     ```tsx
     function VideoCard({ v, assignment, onAssign, onClear }: CardProps) {
       const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
       const [err, setErr] = useState('')
       async function handleAssign(creator: Creator) {
         setSaving(true); setErr('')
         try { await onAssign(creator) } catch (e) { setErr(e instanceof Error ? e.message : 'Failed') }
         setSaving(false)
       }
       // ...
     }
     ```

4. Errors and Fixes:
   - **Build error after adding liveUrl/perfNote to Video type**: `seed.ts` had 13 VideoInput objects missing `liveUrl`. Fixed by adding `liveUrl: ''` to every seed entry.
   - **`netlify dev` port conflict**: `port = 5173` in `[dev]` conflicted with Vite. Fixed: `targetPort = 5173`, `port = 8888`, `framework = "#custom"`.
   - **White screen at 8888 / Vite import-analysis error on 5173**: `[[redirects]]` catch-all `/* -> /index.html` intercepted all requests (including Vite JS module requests) in dev mode through the Netlify proxy. Fixed: moved redirect to `[context.production]` only.
   - **HTTP 403 `API_KEY_HTTP_REFERRER_BLOCKED`**: Debug logging revealed API key still had "HTTP referrers" restriction type (not "None"). Added `Referer` header to outgoing fetch: `headers: { Referer: process.env.SITE_URL ?? 'https://localhost' }`. User also fixed restriction in Google Cloud Console.
   - **`youtube-analytics` returning 500 with no logs**: `YOUTUBE_CHANNEL_ID` env var not set in `.env` file. Fixed: added logging before early returns; user added `YOUTUBE_CHANNEL_ID=UCVYvT-fERO7dQO3QmOlYKBA` to `.env`.
   - **Assignment buttons (PAB/OPHER) doing nothing**: Silent Firestore write failure — `channelVideos` collection rule not deployed to Firebase Console. Also no error handling on the Promise. Fixed: added `saving` state + try/catch with error display in `VideoCard`. User instructed to paste updated rules in Firebase Console.
   - **Unused `reverseMap` variable in Stats.tsx**: TypeScript error `TS6133`. Fixed: removed the unused variable before it was ever used.

5. Problem Solving:
   - **Server-side API key security**: YouTube API key stored as `YOUTUBE_API_KEY` (no VITE_ prefix) so it's never bundled into client JS. Netlify Functions act as a proxy.
   - **Shorts detection without OAuth**: Used `contentDetails.duration` from `videos.list` API, parsed ISO 8601 to seconds. `isShort = secs > 0 && secs <= 60`.
   - **Individual creator stats without extra API calls**: Computed entirely client-side by filtering `uploadedVideos` array by `assignments` map from Firestore subscription.
   - **Creator identity without user profiles**: `creatorFromEmail()` using `VITE_PAB_EMAIL` / `VITE_OPHER_EMAIL` env vars.

[tool_result]
     1→import type { Creator } from '../types/video'
     2→
     3→/**
     4→ * Maps a Firebase Auth email to a creator name using env vars.
     5→ * Add VITE_PAB_EMAIL and VITE_OPHER_EMAIL to your .env.local.
     6→ * Returns null if the email doesn't match either — voting is disabled in that case.
     7→ */
     8→export function creatorFromEmail(email: string | null | undefined): Creator | null {
     9→  if (!email) return null
    10→  if (email === import.meta.env.VITE_PAB_EMAIL)   return 'Pab'
    11→  if (email === import.meta.env.VITE_OPHER_EMAIL) return 'Opher'
    12→  return null
    13→}

[tool_use: Bash]
{
  "command": "python3 -c \"\nimport json, sys\n\npath = '/Users/ophercooper/.claude/projects/-Users-ophercooper-Desktop-Active-Projects-Pabopher-dashboard/30908f61-4880-4e49-b592-afa275ffc44a.jsonl'\nout  = '/Users/ophercooper/Desktop/Active-Projects/Pabopher-dashboard/week-8-full-transcript.txt'\n\nlines = []\nwith open(path) as f:\n    for raw in f:\n        raw = raw.strip()\n        if not raw:\n            continue\n        try:\n            entry = json.loads(raw)\n        except:\n            continue\n\n        msg = entry.get('message', {})\n        role = msg.get('role', '')\n        content = msg.get('content', '')\n\n        if role not in ('user', 'assistant'):\n            continue\n\n        # content can be a string or a list of content blocks\n        if isinstance(content, list):\n            parts = []\n            for block in content:\n                if isinstance(block, dict):\n                    if block.get('type') == 'text':\n                        parts.append(block.get('text', ''))\n                    elif block.get('type') == 'tool_use':\n                        name = block.get('name','')\n                        inp  = json.dumps(block.get('input', {}), indent=2)\n                        parts.append(f'[tool_use: {name}]\\n{inp}')\n                    elif block.get('type') == 'tool_result':\n                        c = block.get('content','')\n                        if isinstance(c, list):\n                            c = ' '.join(b.get('text','') for b in c if isinstance(b,dict))\n                        parts.append(f'[tool_result]\\n{c}')\n            text = '\\n'.join(p for p in parts if p)\n        else:\n            text = str(content)\n\n        label = 'YOU' if role == 'user' else 'CLAUDE'\n        lines.append(f'--- {label} ---\\n{text}\\n')\n\nwith open(out, 'w') as f:\n    f.write('\\n'.join(lines))\n\nprint(f'Done: {len(lines)} messages written to {out}')\n\"\n",
  "description": "Parse JSONL transcript into readable text file"
}
